-----title

-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1fee0a0957bf41fd83ec5516537fe0bd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fee0a0957bf41fd83ec5516537fe0bd");'><span id='1fee0a0957bf41fd83ec5516537fe0bd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>，20岁</div><div id='1fee0a0957bf41fd83ec5516537fe0bd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应真定府路宣抚刘韐募兵备胡，从军为小队长。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>擒农民起义军首领陶俊、贾进和。<br /></div>

-----title
睢阳（宋城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='785b90e5a82643cc8350a34b8b971cec_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("785b90e5a82643cc8350a34b8b971cec");'><span id='785b90e5a82643cc8350a34b8b971cec_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，25岁</div><div id='785b90e5a82643cc8350a34b8b971cec' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年4月24日</a>　从康王至南京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月</a>　上书言事，大忤用事之臣，坐越职夺官。作品：《南京上皇帝书》<div id='poem_1242889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南京上皇帝书略</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242889")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242889'>陛下已登大宝，黎元有归，社稷有主，已足以伐虏人之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242889_comment'></div>而勤王<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242889", 1242889, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>御营</span>之师日集，兵势渐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242889_comment'></div>彼方谓吾素弱，未必能敌，正宜乘其怠而击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242889_comment'></div>而李纲、黄潜善、汪伯彦辈不能承陛下之意，恢复故疆，迎还二圣，奉车驾日益南，又令长安、维扬、襄阳准备巡幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242889_comment'></div>有苟安之渐，无远大之略，恐不足以系中原之望，虽使将帅之臣戮力于外，终亡成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242889_comment'></div>为今之计，莫若请车驾还京，罢三州巡幸之诏，乘二圣蒙尘未久，虏穴未固之际，亲帅六军，迤逦北渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242889_comment'></div>则天威所临，将帅一心，士卒作气，中原之地指期可复。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月18日</a>　诣河北招抚使张所。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月</a>　张所以国士相待，与论用兵及时事。作品：《与张所论用兵及时事》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月</a>　自白身借补修武郎、閤门宣赞舍人、充中军统领。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月</a>　升统制。<br /></div>
-----end

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　收复建康，作申省状。作品：《建康捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建康捷报申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243060")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243060'>武德大夫、英州刺史、御营使下统制岳飞状申：照对飞自建炎三年十一月二十二日起离建康府，至广德军界，与金贼六次见阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243060_comment'></div>收复溧阳县，及于常州界以来邀击金贼，袭逐至镇江府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243060_comment'></div>恭依圣旨，亲提重兵，至建康府，与金贼战斗，追杀过江，收复了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243060_comment'></div>其生擒到伪知溧阳县事、渤海太师李撒八，千户留哥及女真、汉儿等，今差使臣管押申解前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243060_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243060_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2482e233d389466e8d928f3697113d38_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2482e233d389466e8d928f3697113d38");'><span id='2482e233d389466e8d928f3697113d38_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，35岁</div><div id='2482e233d389466e8d928f3697113d38' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月9日</a>　扈从高宗至建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月11日</a>　乞并统淮西兵以复京畿、陕右，许之。命尽护王德等军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月14日</a>　令节制刘光世军，旋作罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　再次上章辞岳云转三官。作品：《辞男云转三官第二札子》<div id='poem_1242962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞男云转三官第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242962")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242962'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣近具奏辞免男云特转三官恩数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242962_comment'></div>今月二日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242962_comment'></div>伏念臣本以凡材，误蒙陛下付以方面，若臣不能与士卒一律，则亦不能整齐其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242962_comment'></div>昨者之战，士卒冒犯矢石，有斩将陷阵，立奇功者，臣方列上事状，得沾一级，而男云何从超进崇资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242962_comment'></div>臣正恐士卒有无功之谤，陛下致滥予之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242962_comment'></div>且陛下方谨惜名器，以磨厉天下，将绍复大业，而乃因臣私恩废公议，臣诚不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242962_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，收还上件恩命，臣父子幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242962_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　第四次上章辞太尉。作品：《辞太尉第四札子》<div id='poem_1242961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞太尉第四劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242961")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242961'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比三具奏，乞追寝恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242961_comment'></div>今月二日准尚书省劄子，二月三十日三省同奉圣旨，依累降诏旨，不允，不得再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242961_comment'></div>臣仰荷圣慈诏谕谆复，然臣实以私情迫切，不容冒进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242961_comment'></div>窃念臣虽无他长，粗知义命，平居服食器用，每安于弊陋，正恐绵薄，不堪禄赐之厚，徒取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242961", 1242961, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>衅眚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242961_comment'></div>臣伏自去春丁家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242961", 1242961, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>忧棘</span>，不复敢有荣官之念，继以目疾，就医至今，其天赋之薄，即此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242961_comment'></div>臣若复尚贪宠数，不自退省，将恐灾疢之来，不特今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242961_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特回天听，收此误恩，全臣知止之节，臣实幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242961_comment'></div>臣叠犯天威，不胜惶惧颠越之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242961_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　上章论恢复之略。作品：《乞出师札子》<div id='poem_1242908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出师劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242908")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242908'>起复太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣自国家变故以来，起于白屋，从陛下于戎伍，实有致身报国、复雠雪耻之心，幸凭社稷威灵，前后粗立薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242908_comment'></div>陛下录臣微劳，擢自布衣，曾未十年，官至太尉，品秩比三公，恩数视二府，又增重使名，宣抚诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242908_comment'></div>臣一介贱微，宠荣超躐，有踰涯分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242908_comment'></div>今者又蒙益臣军马，使济恢图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242908_comment'></div>臣实何能，误辱神圣之知如此，敢不昼度夜思，以图<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>报称</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242908_comment'></div>臣窃揣敌情，所以立刘豫于河南，而付之齐、秦之地，盖欲荼毒中原，以中国而攻中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242908_comment'></div>粘罕因得休兵养马，观衅乘隙，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>包藏</span>不浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242908_comment'></div>臣谓不以此时禀陛下睿算妙略，以伐其谋，使刘豫父子隔绝，五路叛将还归，两河故地渐复，则金人之诡计日生，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>浸益</span>难图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242908_comment'></div>然臣愚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>欲望</span>陛下假臣日月，勿拘其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>淹速</span>，使敌莫测臣之举措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242908_comment'></div>万一得便可入，则提兵直趋京、洛，据河阳、陕府、潼关，以号召五路之叛将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242908_comment'></div>叛将既还，王师前进，彼必舍汴都而走河北，京畿、陕右可以尽复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242908_comment'></div>至于京东诸郡，陛下付之韩世忠、张俊，亦可便下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242908_comment'></div>臣然后分兵浚、滑，经略两河，如此则刘豫父子断必成擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242908_comment'></div>大辽有可立之形，金人有破灭之理，为陛下社稷长久无穷之计，实在此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242908_comment'></div>假令汝、颍、陈、蔡坚壁清野，商于、虢略分屯要害，进或无粮可因，攻或难于馈运，臣须敛兵，还保上流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242908_comment'></div>贼必追袭而南，臣俟其来，当率诸将或挫其锐，或待其疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242908_comment'></div>贼利速战，不得所欲，势必复还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242908_comment'></div>臣当设伏，邀其归路，小入则小胜，大入则大胜，然后徐图再举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242908_comment'></div>设若贼见上流进兵，并力以侵淮上，或分兵犯四川，臣即长驱，捣其巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242908_comment'></div>贼困于奔命，势穷力殚，纵今年未终<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>平殄</span>，来岁必得所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242908_comment'></div>陛下还归旧京，或进都襄阳、关中，唯陛下所择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1242908_comment'></div>臣闻兴师十万，日费千金，内外骚动七十万家，此岂细事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1242908_comment'></div>然古者命将出师，民不再役，粮不再籍，盖虑周而用足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1242908_comment'></div>今臣部曲远在上流，去朝廷数千里，平时每有粮食不足之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1242908_comment'></div>是以去秋臣兵深入陕、洛，而在寨卒伍有饥饿而死者，臣故亟还，前功不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1242908_comment'></div>致使贼地陷伪，忠义之人旋被屠杀，皆臣之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1242908_comment'></div>今日唯赖陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>戒敕</span>有司，广为储备，俾臣得一意静虑，不以兵食乱其方寸，则谋定计审，方能济此大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1242908_comment'></div>异时迎还太上皇帝、宁德皇后梓宫，奉邀天眷，以归故国，使宗庙再安，万姓同欢，陛下高枕万年，无北顾之忧，臣之志愿毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1242908_comment'></div>然后乞身归<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>田里</span>，此臣夙夜所自许者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1242908_comment'></div>臣不胜拳拳孤忠，昧死一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1242908_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1242908", 1242908, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>取进止</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1242908_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　奉诏撰文招降伪齐官吏。作品：《奉诏移伪齐檄》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年4月</a>　诏诣都督府议事，与张浚议不合。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年4月16日</a>　乞解官持余服。<br /></div>
-----end

color: gray;'>▪</span>诏令收复建康。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>复经广德军，于金沙寺壁作题记。作品：《广德军金沙寺壁题记》<div id='poem_1243089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广德军金沙寺壁题记</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243089")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243089'>余驻大兵宜兴，缘干王事过此，陪僧僚谒金仙，徘徊暂憩，遂拥铁骑千馀长驱而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243089_comment'></div>然俟立奇功，殄丑虏，复三关，迎二圣，使宋朝再振，中国安强，他时过此，得勒金石，不胜快哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243089_comment'></div>建炎四年四月十二日，河朔岳飞题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1243089_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dbc7a8e88f904564a98f50216d5c43e7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dbc7a8e88f904564a98f50216d5c43e7");'><span id='dbc7a8e88f904564a98f50216d5c43e7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，28岁</div><div id='dbc7a8e88f904564a98f50216d5c43e7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月14日</a>　平叛将戚方于广德军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2f7505fbe7ee4d1fa0b86e5715871961_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2f7505fbe7ee4d1fa0b86e5715871961");'><span id='2f7505fbe7ee4d1fa0b86e5715871961_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>，36岁</div><div id='2f7505fbe7ee4d1fa0b86e5715871961' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年8月</a>　第三次上章乞致仕。作品：《奏乞致仕第三札子》<br /></div>

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月20日</a>　迁武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使兼知泰州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　以公牍申省，辞通泰之命，愿以母妻并二子为质，乞淮南东路一重难任使。作品：《乞淮东重难任使申省状》<div id='poem_1243031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞淮东重难任使申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243031")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243031'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243031'>武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使、兼知泰州岳飞状申：照得飞近准指挥，差飞充通、泰州镇抚使，仰认朝廷使令之意，除已一面起发，前赴新任外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243031_comment'></div>契勘金贼侵寇虔刘，其志未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243031_comment'></div>要当速行剿杀，殄灭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243031", 1243031, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>静尽</span>，收复诸路，不然则岁月滋久，为患益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243031_comment'></div>若蒙朝廷允飞今来所乞，乞将飞母、妻并二子为质，免充通、泰州镇抚使，止除一淮南东路重难任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243031_comment'></div>令飞招集兵马，掩杀金贼，收复本路州郡，伺便迤逦收复山东、河北、河东、京畿等路故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243031_comment'></div>庶使飞平生之志得以少快，且以尽臣子报君之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243031_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省，伏乞钧慈详察，特赐敷奏，指挥施行，谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243031_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1243031'>〔小贴子〕飞今来所管官兵一面催发前赴新任，如蒙指允飞所乞，即乞速赐指挥，亦不敢仰干朝廷，别求添益军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243031_comment'></div>伏乞钧照<span class='inlineComment2'>（《金佗粹编》卷一七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243031_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1243031'>并二子：原缺，据《金佗粹编》卷五与《金佗续编》卷一四《忠悯谥议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1243031_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　赴泰州任前进言议事。作品：《赴镇画一申省札子》<div id='poem_1243032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴镇画一申省劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243032")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243032'>武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使、兼知泰州岳飞劄子：契勘飞承尚书省劄子，三省、枢密院同奉圣旨，除授通、泰州镇抚使，兼知泰州，今具条画到合行事件下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243032'>一、飞所统人马见在常州宜兴县驻泊，其本县已是阙乏钱粮，无可应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243032_comment'></div>飞见择日起发，前去之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243032_comment'></div>窃闻江阴、镇江见今全阙济渡舟船，兼飞所管官兵老小数多，若以见有舟船装载，半月不能渡绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243032_comment'></div>切虑军兵阙食失所，欲乞于平江府、常州、江阴军等处支拨粮米三、二万硕，应副即目未渡江以前食用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1243032'>一、泰州全藉兴化县在水乡，多收稻谷，以赡兵卒，今蒙已降指挥，从薛庆所乞，隶属承州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243032_comment'></div>泰兴县又已割属扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243032_comment'></div>兼契勘泰州旧有四县，内倚郭海陵附近州城，累遭贼火蹂践，全无所收，如皋一县临于大路，所收不广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243032_comment'></div>今来泰州一小郡，难以却将两县属别州，显于军民妨阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243032_comment'></div>伏望详酌，将上件两县依旧隶属本州，所贵军民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1243032", 1243032, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>通便</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243032_comment'></div>如蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1243032", 1243032, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>许允</span>，乞作特旨行下，恐于人情未便，有妨应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1243032'>一、本军头口，老小、正兵七万馀人口，飞差人前去<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1243032", 1243032, "Clauses/43/Comments/1")'>体探</span>得通、泰二州即目并无粮斛，况粮斛猝急难以擘画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243032_comment'></div>飞体国，不敢过有陈乞支给钱粮，欲乞借支两浙、淮南路盐钞一百万贯，逐旋还纳盐事司，准充盐本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1243032'>一、飞见带军马万馀，自春并不曾支给衣赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243032_comment'></div>今来合给冬衣之时，今体访得通、泰州即目钱帛阙少，本州人兵尚无可支散，切虑因此失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243032_comment'></div>伏望详酌体念，特赐于有钱绢官司或别州军去处支给冬衣一次，贵免官兵赤露失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1243032'>右谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1243032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月19日</a>　诏以所部救楚州，发宜兴。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
兴化（海陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='012d7483e5a1422299a0de973a76f083_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("012d7483e5a1422299a0de973a76f083");'><span id='012d7483e5a1422299a0de973a76f083_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，28岁</div><div id='012d7483e5a1422299a0de973a76f083' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月9日</a>　屯驻三墩以援楚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月</a>　作状向刘光世安抚使司乞兵马食粮。作品：《申刘光世乞兵马食粮状》<div id='poem_1243033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申刘光世乞兵马粮食状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243033")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243033'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243033'>武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使、兼知泰州岳飞状申：飞昨奉圣旨指挥，差充前件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243033_comment'></div>于八月十五日还至常州宜兴县，于十八日起发前来，祗赴新任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243033_comment'></div>二十二日至江阴军歇泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243033_comment'></div>据探报，金人见围楚州，飞遂逐急权差统制王贵管押兵马，等船济渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243033_comment'></div>切虑迟滞，有失事机，不免躬亲先入泰州，于二十六日夜二更到泰州城外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243033_comment'></div>承准八月十九日指挥，令飞与赵镇抚立掎角，飞遂措置调发兵夫、粮食，并不住差人勾唤王贵等军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243033_comment'></div>实缘舟船数少，今月初九日，方尽到泰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243033_comment'></div>飞已差张宪权行守城，见今大军屯驻三墩，与金人大寨不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243033_comment'></div>惟是新复建康之后，所有士马疮痍尚新，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1243033", 1243033, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>羸弊</span>方甚，兼自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1243033", 1243033, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>到任</span>未及一旬，刍茭、糗粮一一窘乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243033_comment'></div>本未能即从王事，重以承、楚之急，甚于倒垂，不可以顷刻安居，理宜前进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243033_comment'></div>欲望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1243033", 1243033, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'>钧慈</span>捐一、二千之众，假十馀日之粮，令飞得激厉士卒，径赴贼垒，解二州之围，扫犬羊之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243033_comment'></div>下以裨相公之盛烈，上以宽主上之深忧，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243033_comment'></div>谨具申安抚相公使司，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1243033_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月</a>　高宗赐札令与刘光世所遣协力并进，作状请战。作品：《申刘光世进兵状》<div id='poem_1243034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申刘光世乞进兵状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243034")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243034'>武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使、兼知泰州岳飞状申：窃念飞以行伍贱隶，辱知朝廷，蒙被厚恩，殒没难报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243034_comment'></div>每以为国家之难，虽非所命，犹当戮力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243034_comment'></div>矧承、楚之事，危迫如许，累准朝廷指挥催督，此正飞等<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243034", 1243034, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>捐身徇义</span>之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243034_comment'></div>切缘王镇抚林、郭镇抚仲威等并不见差拨军马前来，使司王统制虽闻已起发，即目尚未知屯驻去处，使飞孤军委实难以支梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243034_comment'></div>今月十二日，准本州递到今月六日指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243034_comment'></div>飞除已遵禀外，契勘金贼盘泊日久，连破诸镇，王镇抚、郭镇抚等各敛兵自保，其志已骄，目即承、楚一带民户逃死，别无卤掠，易于攻却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243034_comment'></div>据探报，虏人急攻楚州，切恐万一疏虞，于淮南诸镇利害不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243034_comment'></div>飞已于今月十五日具申使司去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243034_comment'></div>飞一面起发，前往承州以来，措置剿杀外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243034_comment'></div>伏乞钧慈特捐一、二千之众，别差统制官一员前来掎角，庶立大功，不致上误国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243034_comment'></div>谨具申安抚相公使司，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1243034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年10月26日</a>　破金人于承州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年10月</a>　献俘行在，并作状申尚书省并枢院。作品：《承州捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>承州捷报申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243061")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243061'>武功大夫、昌州防御使、通泰州镇抚使、兼知泰州岳飞状申：恭依指挥，选精锐分头会合，及率人马直抵承州，掩杀金贼，三次见阵获捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243061_comment'></div>所有逐次生擒女真、契丹、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243061", 1243061, "Clauses/6/Comments/3")'>渤海</span>、汉儿军高太保等，除身死外，见管女真三人：阿主里孛堇、白打里、蒲速里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243061_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243061", 1243061, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>渤海</span>一名：李用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243061_comment'></div>契丹一名：毛毛可𣸭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243061_comment'></div>奚人三人：王哥、合主、留哥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243061_comment'></div>汉儿一十二人：李延寿、赵月一、张大、李兴门、侯孝兴、解德、小儿、麻大、曹黑儿、杨四儿、杨章儿、孙公仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243061_comment'></div>今差使臣某人管押申解前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243061_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年10月</a>　帝赐札褒奖。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
祁门
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='aa9ae9b5c53049a6b7bd96536c19dd2a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa9ae9b5c53049a6b7bd96536c19dd2a");'><span id='aa9ae9b5c53049a6b7bd96536c19dd2a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>，29岁</div><div id='aa9ae9b5c53049a6b7bd96536c19dd2a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年2月14日</a>　自江阴至鄱阳途中，游东松寺，有文。作品：《东松寺题记》<div id='poem_1243090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东松寺题记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年2月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243090")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243090'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243090'>余自江阴军提兵起发，前赴饶郡，与张招讨会合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243090_comment'></div>崎岖山路，殆及千里，过祁门西约一舍馀，当途有庵一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243090_comment'></div>问其僧，曰「东松」，遂邀后军王团练并幕属随嬉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243090_comment'></div>观其基址，乃凿山开地，创立廊庑，三山环耸，势凌碧落，万木森郁，密掩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243090", 1243090, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>烟甍</span>，胜景潇洒，实为可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243090_comment'></div>所恨不能款曲，进程遄速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243090_comment'></div>俟他日殄灭盗贼，凯旋回归，复得至此，即当聊结善缘，以慰庵僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243090_comment'></div>绍兴改元仲春十有四日，河朔岳飞题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243090_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

南昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年3月</a>　钱粮缺乏，致某郎中乞请。作品：《致某郎中乞粮书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《岳飞集辑注》原注为本年九月。据文中“比至豫章”，知为岳飞初到洪州之时作，当与《致某通判书》乞营寨作于同时。故改系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年3月9日</a>　与张俊、杨沂中渡赣江击马进，败之于西山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8a3632bf57464d82a3e4fb20fd0d01eb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a3632bf57464d82a3e4fb20fd0d01eb");'><span id='8a3632bf57464d82a3e4fb20fd0d01eb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年6月18日</a>　招降叛将张用，江淮悉平。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月6日</a>　充神武右副军统制，权留洪州，弹压盗贼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月</a>　游览洪州西山翠岩寺，有题诗。作品：《题翠岩寺》<div id='poem_166922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题翠岩寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_166922")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_166922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166922'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166922'>秋风江上驻王师，暂向云山蹑翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166922'>忠义必期清塞水，功名直欲镇边圻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166922'>山林啸聚何劳取，沙漠群凶定破机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_166922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_166922'>行复三关迎二圣，金酋席卷尽擒归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_166922'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_166922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_166922'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(166922)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年10月</a>　授亲卫大夫建州观察使，讨建州范汝为起义军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月4日</a>　作札乞拨钱粮。作品：《乞科拨钱粮照会从申省札》<div id='poem_1243071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞科拨钱粮照会从申省劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243071")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243071'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243071'>契勘飞于绍兴元年八月十三日，准枢密院劄子，备奉圣旨指挥，令飞一行官兵权留洪州驻劄，弹压盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243071_comment'></div>续奉圣旨指挥，般取本军昨存留徽州官兵老小，前来洪州一处屯泊，合用钱粮令江西转运司应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243071_comment'></div>寻不住移牒本司，据本军合用钱粮，恭依已降圣旨指挥，应副施行去后，并不见措置科拨催发到来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243071_comment'></div>况本军方到洪州驻劄一月馀日，累承本州公文，止称阙乏，应办不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243071_comment'></div>其合勘请十月初五日至初九日钱米，除已支请外，少钱五千四百九十六贯七百五十文、米七百四十一石三斗一升五合，支遣不足，所有初九日已后钱米亦无指准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243071_comment'></div>念飞所部军兵唯仰官给钱粮，养赡过日，方免失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243071_comment'></div>似此洪州并不挂意，着紧措画，移那应副，及江西转运司又不见预行宽剩计置，取拨赴洪州，相续支用，致得阙误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243071_comment'></div>不唯军兵自即已见阙食，兼日后又无指准批请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243071_comment'></div>自今年九月二十三日后来，不住申明朝廷，乞赐行下本路转运司，疾早措置，支移合用钱粮，起发前来洪州，应副支遣去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243071_comment'></div>至今未蒙回降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243071_comment'></div>除已具录奏闻，伏望圣慈特降睿旨，下江西转运司，将本军合用钱粮，着紧催发，相继津般前来，以济急阙支用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243071_comment'></div>及令洪州更切多方计置，移那应副施行，庶免冬月官兵阙食失所外，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1243071_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6dba8f09b61f46d4a526c791121b4074_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6dba8f09b61f46d4a526c791121b4074");'><span id='6dba8f09b61f46d4a526c791121b4074_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1132')">1131-1132年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='6dba8f09b61f46d4a526c791121b4074' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年12月14日</a>　为神武副军都统制，仍以所部屯洪州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月29日</a>　诏权知潭州兼权荆湖东路安抚使、都总管。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月8日</a>　诏讨贼曹成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月</a>　讨曹成前作状申状。作品：《申审招安申省状》<div id='poem_1243035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申审招安申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243035")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243035'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞申：契勘湖东路见今盗贼啸聚，动以数万，李宏在岳州，刘忠在湘阴，曹成在道州作过，其馀寇盗不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243035_comment'></div>除见措置剿杀外，其间若有能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243035", 1243035, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>改行自新</span>之人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243035", 1243035, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>未委</span>合与不合招安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243035_comment'></div>如许飞招安，欲望给降金字牌、黄旗十副，仍乞差使臣管押，付飞交割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243035_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1243035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月17日</a>　发洪州。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月</a>　始成军，独挡一面。作词抒报国心志。作品：《满江红》（怒发冲冠）<div id='poem_166925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 写怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_166925")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_166925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166925'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166925'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_166925", 166925, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>怒发冲冠</span>，凭阑处、潇潇雨歇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166925'>抬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_166925", 166925, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>望眼</span>、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_166925", 166925, "Clauses/2/Comments/2")'>仰天</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_166925", 166925, "Clauses/2/Comments/3")'>长啸</span>，壮怀激烈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166925'>三十<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_166925", 166925, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>功名</span>尘与土，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_166925", 166925, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>八千里路云和月</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_166925'>莫等閒、白了少年头，空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_166925", 166925, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>悲切</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166925_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_166925'>靖康耻，犹未雪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_166925'>臣子恨，何时灭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_166925'>驾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_166925", 166925, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>长车</span>踏破，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_166925", 166925, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>贺兰山</span>缺。<div id='poem_sentence_6_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_166925'>壮志饥餐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_166925", 166925, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>胡虏</span>肉，笑谈渴饮匈奴血。<div id='poem_sentence_7_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_166925'>待从头、收拾旧山河，朝天阙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_166925'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_166925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_166925'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(166925)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年12月</a>　李横等失守襄阳等地，无所归，上奏请求处置。作品：《措置李横等军奏》<div id='poem_1242895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置李横等军奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242895")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242895'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州制置使臣岳飞状奏：契勘襄阳府李横、郢州李刺史、翟镇抚、董先、随州李道、牛皋等逐头项军马例各失守，将带到百姓随行，见无所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242895_comment'></div>臣虽非所职，缘事干国计，不敢隐默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242895_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，令李横、李刺史、翟镇抚、董先人马于汉阳军屯驻，李道、牛皋人马于黄州或依旧蕲州屯驻，且令安集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242895_comment'></div>仍乞令李横等将百姓放令逐便，庶免转沦沟壑之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242895_comment'></div>候屯驻定，却听朝廷指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242895_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1242895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年12月</a>　奏请李道等人马听其节制。作品：《奏审李道牛皋军奏》<div id='poem_1242896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏审李道牛皋军奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242896")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242896'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州制置使臣岳飞状奏：契勘李道、牛皋人马累得申状，乞听臣节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242896_comment'></div>臣以未准朝旨，不敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242896", 1242896, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>拘收</span>，见且令前来江州权行驻劄外，伏望特降睿旨，令系属一处节制，庶几军律有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242896_comment'></div>如蒙付臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242896", 1242896, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>拘收</span>使唤，亦乞行下，恭依施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242896_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年12月14日</a>　诏李横、翟琮、董先、李道、牛皋并听节制，以图后效。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月</a>　上书乞复襄阳。作品：《乞复襄阳札子》<div id='poem_1242897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞复襄阳劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242897")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242897'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242897'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣窃惟善观敌者，当逆知其所始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242897_comment'></div>善制敌者，当先去其所恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242897_comment'></div>今外有北虏之寇攘，内有杨么之窃发，俱为大患，上轸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242897", 1242897, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>宸襟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242897_comment'></div>然以臣观之，杨么虽近为腹心之忧，其实外假李成，以为唇齿之援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242897_comment'></div>今日之计，正当进兵襄阳，先取六郡，李成不就絷缚，则亦丧师远逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242897_comment'></div>于是加兵湖湘，以殄群盗，要不为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242897_comment'></div>而况襄阳六郡，地为险要，恢复中原，此为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242897", 1242897, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>基本</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242897_comment'></div>臣今已厉兵饬士，惟俟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1242897", 1242897, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>报可</span>，指期北向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242897_comment'></div>伏乞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242897", 1242897, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>睿断</span>，速赐施行，庶几上流早见平定，中兴之功次第而致，不胜天下之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242897_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1242897_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1242898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画守襄阳等郡劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242898")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242898'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣六月二十三日酉时，准御前金字牌，伏蒙圣慈特降亲札处分，令臣条具襄阳、随、郢利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242898_comment'></div>臣窃观金贼、刘豫皆有可取之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242898_comment'></div>金贼累年之间，贪婪横逆，无所不至，今所爱惟金帛、子女，志已骄堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242898_comment'></div>刘豫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>僭臣</span>贼子，虽以俭约结民，而人心终不忘宋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242898_comment'></div>攻讨之谋，正不宜缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242898_comment'></div>苟岁月迁延，使得修治<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>城壁</span>，添兵聚粮，而后取之，必倍费力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242898_comment'></div>陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>渊谋远略</span>，非臣所知，以臣自料，如及此时，以精兵二十万直捣中原，恢复故疆，民心效顺，诚易为力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242898_comment'></div>此则国家长久之策也，在陛下睿断耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242898_comment'></div>若姑以目前论之，襄阳、随、郢地皆膏腴，民力不支，苟行营田之法，其利为厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242898_comment'></div>然即今将已七月，未能耕垦，来年入春，即可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>措画</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242898_comment'></div>陛下欲驻大兵于鄂州，则襄阳、随、郢量留军马，又于安、复、汉阳亦量驻兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242898_comment'></div>兵势相援，漕运相继，荆门、荆南声援亦已相接，江、淮、荆湖皆可奠安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242898_comment'></div>六州之屯，且以正兵六万，为固守之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242898_comment'></div>就拨江西、湖南粮斛，朝廷支降券钱，为一年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>支遣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242898_comment'></div>候营田就绪，军储既成，则朝廷无馈饷之忧，进攻退守，皆兼利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242898_comment'></div>惟是葺治之初，未免艰难，必仰朝廷微有以资之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242898_comment'></div>基本既立，后之利源无有穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242898_comment'></div>又此地夏秋则江水涨隔，外可以御寇，内足以运粮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242898_comment'></div>至冬后春初，江水浅涩，吾资粮已备，可以坐待矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242898_comment'></div>于今所先，在乎速备粮食，斟量屯守之兵，可善其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242898_comment'></div>臣识闇不学，辄具管见，仰报圣问，辞拙事直，伏乞圣慈裁决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1242898_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣不胜屏营战慄之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1242898_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1242898_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1242898'>〔贴黄〕臣见今只候粮食稍足，即便过江北，虽番、伪贼马势重，臣定竭力剿戮，不敢少负陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1242898_comment'></div>伏乞特宽宵旰之念，不胜庆幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1242898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月10日</a>　命吴锡率所部自鄂州南下平南丹蛮之乱，作诗送行。作品：《宝刀歌书赠吴将军南行》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='825b56b43373424caf05b6ea61632234_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("825b56b43373424caf05b6ea61632234");'><span id='825b56b43373424caf05b6ea61632234_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，34岁</div><div id='825b56b43373424caf05b6ea61632234' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年4月</a>　上章乞寝罢格外赙赠。作品：《辞母亡格外赙赠及应办丧事奏》<div id='poem_1242950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞母亡格外赙赠及应办丧事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242950")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242950'>草土臣岳飞状奏：臣准御前金字牌递到尚书省劄子二道，奉圣旨，岳飞母身亡，已降指挥起复，于格外特赐银、绢一千匹两，令户部支给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242950_comment'></div>所有葬事，令鄂州协力措置施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242950_comment'></div>臣上荷圣恩，惟知感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242950_comment'></div>契勘臣今般挈家属，扶护母丧，已至江州瑞昌县，择定江州界营葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242950_comment'></div>臣以月俸之馀，粗足办集，所有上件恩数并格外赙赠，伏望圣慈并赐寝罢，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242950_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1242950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年4月8日</a>　诏起复，遣使抚问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年4月12日</a>　上章为母守丧。作品：《乞终制札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年4月29日</a>　诏仍兼节制蕲黄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年5月1日</a>　再上章为母守制。作品：《乞终制第二札子》<div id='poem_1242953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞终制第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242953")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242953'>草土臣岳飞劄子奏：准枢密院劄子，勘会臣母魏国太夫人姚氏身故，已降指挥起复，仍日下主管军马职事，不得辞免，仍具已供职月日闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242953_comment'></div>臣契勘除已具辞免奏闻外，伏望圣慈检会所奏，特许臣终制。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242952_comment'></div>今月初一日，准御前金字牌递到尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242952_comment'></div>伏念臣遭遇圣眷，过于山岳，感激之心，惟极涕泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242952_comment'></div>今已安葬了当，种种办集，皆自陛下恩被之所及，所有前项银、绢实难重叠祗拜，伏望特赐寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242952_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年5月</a>　第三次上章为母守制。作品：《乞终制第三札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注谓五月初一日有《乞终制第三札子》，据文意当误，应为第二札子。）</span><div id='poem_1242954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞终制第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242954")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242954'>草土臣岳飞劄子奏：近于四月十二日具奏，辞免起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242954_comment'></div>今月初一日，准御前金字牌递到尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，不允，令学士院降诏，仍不得再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242954_comment'></div>依已降指挥，日下主管军马，措置调发，不管少失机会者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242954_comment'></div>伏念臣叨荷圣恩，实倍伦等，惟期尽忠，庶图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242954_comment'></div>缘臣老母沦亡，忧苦号泣，两目遂昏，方寸亦多健忘，自揆馀生，岂复尚堪器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242954_comment'></div>非敢独孝于亲，而于陛下不竭其忠，正谓灾屯如此，不能任事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242954_comment'></div>况臣一介<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242954", 1242954, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>右列</span>，若学术稍优，谋略可取，亦当勉强措置调发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242954_comment'></div>臣于二者俱乏所长，今既眼目昏眊，又不能身先士卒，贾作锐气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242954_comment'></div>苟不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242954", 1242954, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>罄沥</span>血诚，披告陛下，则他日必致颠隮，上辜委寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242954_comment'></div>伏望睿慈俯察孤衷，许臣终制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242954_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1242954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
茶陵
-----detail

href='/Writing/1243037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>分拣吴锡韩京两军讫申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243037")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243037'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞申：契勘飞近奉圣旨，差权荆湖东路安抚、都总管，及统率马友并本路李宏、吴锡、韩京诸头项军马，前来措置掩杀曹成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243037_comment'></div>飞寻依应起发，已到湖东界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243037_comment'></div>其韩京元屯兵衡州茶陵县，吴锡在郴州，两项所管官兵多是老弱，及湖东土人在内充数，其实堪出战人各不满一千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243037_comment'></div>又缘不经战斗，久在州县屯泊，全无纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243037_comment'></div>今来飞已将上件人马，除拣选不堪披带人给据放散外，将实堪披带人数分拨付本军诸将收管使唤讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243037_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　斟酌曹成动向，上奏应对举措。作品：《措置曹成事宜奏》<div id='poem_1242892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置曹成事宜奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242892")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242892'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管臣岳飞状奏：四月初二日，准江南西路安抚大使司牒，三月二十三日，准枢密院三月四日劄子：「奉圣旨，令岳飞到袁州，更切斟量贼势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242892_comment'></div>如贼兵众，且于袁州驻劄，俟宣抚司人马到，同共进兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242892_comment'></div>如曹成已受招安，起发赴行在，即与马友会合，同共剿杀刘忠讫，续往潭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242892_comment'></div>飞素有谋略，毋致稍失机会，却致贼兵破坏二广」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242892_comment'></div>臣检会绍兴二年二月八日枢密院劄子节文：「曹成贼马占据道、贺州作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242892_comment'></div>三省、枢密院同奉圣旨，令宣抚司催督高举，星夜前去应援二广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242892_comment'></div>及令荆湖东路安抚使岳飞统率副总管马友，并本路李宏、吴锡、韩京诸头项军马，火急前去，袭逐掩击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242892_comment'></div>其马友等并听帅臣岳飞节制，各务<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>体国</span>，共力破贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242892_comment'></div>仍仰广东、西路帅臣起发逐路洞丁、刀弩手、将兵、土军、弓手、民兵，疾速躬亲统率前去逐路界首，与岳飞会合，并力夹击，务要一举万全」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242892_comment'></div>臣已即时关报会合马友、吴锡、韩京等军马，及牒广东、西路安抚使统率本路洞丁、刀弩手等，各前来界首会合照应，夹击剿杀外，臣一行军马已到衡州茶陵县，不住承准郴州、桂阳监等处关报，及臣亦差人体探得曹成发人马，取三月十九日起发，往全、永州，侵犯广西界分，并前军人马往贺州路前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242892_comment'></div>其曹成中军见在道州，未有的实起发月日，不住放人四向虏掠，杀人放火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242892_comment'></div>似此显见曹成未肯便赴行在，意欲侵犯二广作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242892_comment'></div>今准前项江南西路安抚大使李回公牒，备奉前项圣旨指挥，一行官兵已过袁州，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>地里</span>稍远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242892_comment'></div>兼续于四月初三日，准荆湖东路提刑司关报，曹成贼马已起发，离道州，前去广西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242892_comment'></div>除已差人体探子细外，今已进发往郴州、桂阳监以来驻泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242892_comment'></div>如曹成不赴行在，及入广西，臣便行措置进兵掩杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242892_comment'></div>若曹成已入广界，不审令臣一行军马如何施行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242892_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨付臣，贵凭遵依施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242892_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242892_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1242892'>〔贴黄〕照对臣所统本军官兵一万二千馀人，除存留二千人吉州看管老小，并随军辎重、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/76/Comments/1")'>火头</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/76/Comments/2")'>占破</span>外，实出战只有七千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242892_comment'></div>吴全二千人，除辎重、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/79/Comments/1")'>火头</span>外，实出战一千五百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1242892_comment'></div>韩京三千人，除留看寨、辎重、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1242892", 1242892, "Clauses/82/Comments/2")'>火头</span>外，堪出战只有一千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1242892_comment'></div>吴锡约二千馀人，堪出战有一千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1242892_comment'></div>张中彦人马见在广东未到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1242892_comment'></div>今来共计见有实出战官兵一万馀人，所有曹成贼寇仅十万众，臣已竭力措置外，伏望圣慈速令并进后援，庶使臣无反顾之忧，得以有济，伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1242892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　招曹成不果，上札主张用兵。作品：《招曹成不成乞进兵札子》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='90d8da44725742dbab7b45b176a1fb35_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("90d8da44725742dbab7b45b176a1fb35");'><span id='90d8da44725742dbab7b45b176a1fb35_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，30岁</div><div id='90d8da44725742dbab7b45b176a1fb35' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　至郴州永兴界追赶曹成，作申省状。作品：《乞措置进兵入广申省状》<div id='poem_1243036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞措置进兵入广申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243036")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243036'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞申：契勘飞承枢密院劄子，奉圣旨指挥，统率军马前来湖东，措置收捕曹成贼马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243036_comment'></div>飞寻依时起发，及沿路不住差信实人到道州以来，体探上件曹成作为次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243036_comment'></div>至三月三十日，游兵到衡州茶陵县，承诸处探报，曹成已于三月二十七日起离道州，望全、永州路前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243036_comment'></div>缘茶陵县至道州尚有六百馀里，飞未敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243036", 1243036, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>信凭</span>，遂领一行军马前来郴州、桂阳监，体度贼马的实动息，于四月初八日到郴州管下永兴界，地名橘水郊，承郴州并桂阳监公文，探知曹成贼马分路逃遁，前去全、永、贺州界去讫，至三月二十七日并已起离道州尽绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243036_comment'></div>本军亦差人探得，与诸处关报一同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243036_comment'></div>飞今部领军马，前去道州，如到彼贼兵未远，即便尾袭追赶，若逃遁程途已远，其贼闻飞兵到，必不敢前来拒敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243036_comment'></div>飞欲深往追赶，又恐二广不曾得朝廷指挥，不肯应办钱粮，必致阙误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243036_comment'></div>兼近据潭州申，刘忠掩杀马友下统制王成大溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243036_comment'></div>窃恐马友见飞已入湖东，及曹成遁走，又不能捍御刘忠贼马，以此心怀疑惑，别致生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243036_comment'></div>飞欲径往潭州，安抚马友讫，先次措置剿杀刘忠等贼了当，即乞前去收捕曹成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243036_comment'></div>除已具录奏闻外，伏望特降指挥，付飞遵依施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243036_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243036_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1243036'>〔小贴子〕飞契勘曹成贼马经由全、永、贺州界逃遁，已不住关报广东、西安抚使，请为统率逐路军马，照应把截，无致侵入二广外，伏望特降指挥，下逐路帅臣，更切火急严紧把截施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243036_comment'></div>伏候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243036_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1243036'>〔又小贴子〕契勘湖东事体非轻，飞出自寒微，望轻材薄，今令权一路，切恐不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1243036", 1243036, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>称任</span>，止乞依旧统制名目，前去追杀曹成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243036_comment'></div>仍乞先次行下二广路，令应副一行钱粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243036_comment'></div>仍乞一才干官，充随军运使，专一措置钱粮，庶得常不阙误。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1243036_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
贺州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='886e7cfc33524e5fa25d9b965d8d7515_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("886e7cfc33524e5fa25d9b965d8d7515");'><span id='886e7cfc33524e5fa25d9b965d8d7515_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，30岁</div><div id='886e7cfc33524e5fa25d9b965d8d7515' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月6日</a>　破曹成于贺州境，作申省状。作品：《贺州捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺州捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年闰4月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243062")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243062'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞状申：闰四月六日，飞进兵离贺州二十馀里，曹成贼兵三万馀人占据山险，迎敌官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243062_comment'></div>即时鼓率士卒掩杀，贼兵败走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243062_comment'></div>飞又率兵追至贺州城东江岸，其贼望桂岭路逃遁前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243062_comment'></div>飞寻勾本军离贺州二十馀里下寨，并不曾放人入城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243062_comment'></div>贺州钱粮系广西经略安抚许中下统制欧阳临、罗选等差丁兵占守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243062_comment'></div>所有飞一行军马只沿路就贼粮斛食用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243062_comment'></div>飞见行进兵，前去桂岭县，破灭曹成大队次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243062_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243062_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月</a>　乞拨战马追击曹成，作申省状。作品：《乞广西战马申省状》<div id='poem_1243038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞广西战马申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年闰4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243038")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243038'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞状申：恭奉圣旨指挥，差拨飞军马前来，措置收捕曹成贼马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243038_comment'></div>其曹成近自道州起发，部领贼众，于贺州界深山桂岭劄立巢穴，占据<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243038", 1243038, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>崄峻</span>，备敌官军，飞提兵到北藏岭下寨，其贼严备守隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243038_comment'></div>飞料曹成骑兵颇多，缘飞所管战马，比之曹成，数目十不及一，遂逐急于广西经略司省马内借到三百匹，乘骑出战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243038_comment'></div>与曹成下王渊贼马<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243038", 1243038, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>见阵</span>，约及数时，杀散王渊了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243038_comment'></div>其所借省马为自广西远来，料食不足，例皆疲瘦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243038_comment'></div>及<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1243038", 1243038, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>见阵</span>，往来驰逐，落崖倒死者一百八十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243038_comment'></div>伏望特降指挥，将上件见管未还广西马数特许存留，充神武副军出战，及更乞下广西经略司支拨堪好马五百匹，付飞使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243038_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月16日</a>　败曹成于桂岭县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月</a>　曹成窜入广东、湖南、江西，遣将持续追击，作申省状。作品：《追赶曹成捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追赶曹成捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年闰4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243064")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243064'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞状申：恭奉圣旨，收捕曹成贼马，于今年闰四月五日绕岭沿路掩杀，破荡巢穴了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243064_comment'></div>其曹成奔窜广东连州，遂遣本司统制官张宪追赶掩杀，收复连州了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243064_comment'></div>曹成已入湖南，望江西逃窜，并曹成先发都统领王渊贼马望桂阳监路前去，寻遣本司统制官王贵追赶杀散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243064_comment'></div>其馀徒党望江西散走，贼势大段穷蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243064_comment'></div>飞除已躬亲提兵剿杀招收外，飞契勘捉到曹成下将官张全等通说，曹成军中实有河北、河东、山东、京畿、陕西等七万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243064_comment'></div>飞自今年闰四月五日后来，节次杀戮，约及太半，平荡指日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243064_comment'></div>伏恐庙堂过忧，上勤宵旰，谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞敷奏施行，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月21日</a>　平定曹成，作申省状。作品：《大破曹成捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大破曹成捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243063")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243063'>亲卫大夫、建州观察使、神武副军都统制、权知潭州、兼权荆湖东路安抚、都总管岳飞状申：准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，收捕曹成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243063_comment'></div>除于今年闰四月五日，自绕岭路下手，掩杀曹成下把隘并<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243063", 1243063, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>游掠</span>贼兵，破荡州界太平场贼寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243063_comment'></div>当月六日，离贺州二十馀里，杀散曹成下贼兵三万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243063_comment'></div>十二日，杀散北藏岭、上梧关守隘贼兵，占夺关口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243063_comment'></div>十三日，杀散曹成发来照应北藏岭，夹击官军贼兵一万五千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243063_comment'></div>除已具杀获次第，捉杀人数，夺到弓箭枪刀等申枢密院外，飞契勘曹成自桂岭县劄立大寨，至北藏岭约六十馀里，尽是山险河涧，唯狭路往来，人马不得并行，兼北藏岭、上梧关、蓬岭三隘所阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243063_comment'></div>已取夺北藏岭、上梧关两隘了当，至闰四月十五日，进兵蓬岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243063_comment'></div>其贼严备隘口，把截官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243063_comment'></div>飞于当日未时以来，分布兵将，一拥上岭，与贼战敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243063_comment'></div>其贼大败，四向奔溃，杀死及掩拥入河不知其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243063_comment'></div>十六日，取桂岭县，取夺大寨了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243063_comment'></div>其曹成带领残零溃贼，望连州路逃窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243063_comment'></div>夺到枪刀、金鼓、旗帜不计数目，及夺到被虏人民数万人，放令归业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243063_comment'></div>飞见遣四向搜逻剿戮，追袭杀捕，并关报广东经略把截，乘势掩杀外，谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月9日</a>　诏屯驻江州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月11日</a>　以破曹成功，迁中卫大夫武安军承宣使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
祁阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ff063a09be984f3e8b65350b2d0d9057_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ff063a09be984f3e8b65350b2d0d9057");'><span id='ff063a09be984f3e8b65350b2d0d9057_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，30岁</div><div id='ff063a09be984f3e8b65350b2d0d9057' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月7日</a>　破曹成后，过祁阳大营驿，题壁言志。作品：《题永州祁阳县大营驿》<div id='poem_1243091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州祁阳县大营驿题记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243091")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243091'>权湖南帅岳飞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1243091", 1243091, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>被旨</span>讨贼曹成，自桂岭平荡巢穴，二广、湖湘悉皆安妥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243091_comment'></div>痛念二圣远狩沙漠，天下靡宁，誓竭忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243091_comment'></div>赖社稷威灵，君相贤圣，他日扫清胡虏，复归故国，迎两宫还朝，宽天子宵旰之忧，此所志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243091_comment'></div>顾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243091", 1243091, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>蜂蚁</span>之群，岂足为功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243091_comment'></div>过此，因留于壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243091_comment'></div>绍兴二年七月初七日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243091_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
于都（雩都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3ffd68ccccda49cb87ec54f4a21eeb15_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ffd68ccccda49cb87ec54f4a21eeb15");'><span id='3ffd68ccccda49cb87ec54f4a21eeb15_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年4月</a>　至雩都县罗田岩华岩寺游，有题诗。作品：《题雩都华岩寺》<div id='poem_166913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题雩都华严寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166913'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166913'>手持竹节访黄龙，旧穴空遗虎子踪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166913'>云锁断崖无觅处，半山松竹撼秋风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166913'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年4月</a>　破雩都石固洞，虔吉起义军悉平。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年5月</a>　擒虔州起义军诸首领，奏请处置。作品：《奏审虔州贼首奏》<div id='poem_1242894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏审虔州贼首奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242894")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242894'>中卫大夫、武安军承宣使、神武副军都统制臣岳飞状奏：恭奉圣旨，措置虔贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242894_comment'></div>今已节次生擒杀降到虔州诸县界山寨贼首罗诚等二百馀人，见拘管在寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242894_comment'></div>未审令臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242894", 1242894, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>一面</span>处置，唯复申解朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242894_comment'></div>伏望圣慈速赐指挥，以凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242894", 1242894, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>遵禀</span>施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242894_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年5月</a>　平虔州叛乱，作申省状。作品：《虔州捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虔州捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243065")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243065'>中卫大夫、武安军承宣使、神武副军都统制岳飞状申：契勘恭奉亲札处分，措置虔州等处盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243065_comment'></div>飞准江南宣谕牒，据吉州龙泉县申：「本县被贼人彭友、李动天结集头领凶贼，伪称十大王，已经四年，攻破八县，大段猖獗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243065_comment'></div>其彭友等贼徒见在本县界武陵、烈源、陈田三处劄寨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243065_comment'></div>飞恭依圣旨，先差使臣赍文字前去招谕，其伪十大王彭友等八头项并不肯听从，又结集永新县界群贼尹花八等二项贼徒三千馀人等，迎敌官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243065_comment'></div>飞分遣统领官张宪取一路，王贵取一路，飞躬亲统率军马取一路，约期会合迎敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243065_comment'></div>其贼沿山摆布，飞遂率将士战斗，当日贼众败走下山，夺到隘口数处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243065_comment'></div>飞躬亲督率军马，分头下山，与贼战斗，杀死贼徒遍满山谷，并枪牌、衣甲等，及夺救到被虏老小二万馀人，已放令逐便，具录奏闻外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243065_comment'></div>飞续遣兵于山村搜杀不尽残党，捉到贼魁伪十大王彭友、李满并以次头领，随军监防外，谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243065_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b6df16cef5304451a7dc2bf36a1734ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b6df16cef5304451a7dc2bf36a1734ce");'><span id='b6df16cef5304451a7dc2bf36a1734ce_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月15日</a>　落阶官，为镇南军承宣使江南西路沿江制置使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月</a>　上章辞免镇南军承宣使。作品：《辞镇南军承宣使第三奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（前两奏已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞镇南军承宣使第三奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242931")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242931'>中卫大夫、武安军承宣使、神武副军都统制臣岳飞状奏：臣今月十五日准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，除臣正任承宣使，充江南西路沿江制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242931_comment'></div>臣已两具辞免，伏蒙圣慈降诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242931_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242931", 1242931, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>荣命</span>下颁，惊魂顿失，辞章上达，帝命不俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242931_comment'></div>虽臣受之不惭，恐舆情之未协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242931_comment'></div>辄陈恳愊，方切忧惶，复蒙天语之丁宁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242931", 1242931, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>告戒</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242931", 1242931, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>备至</span>，愈使臣心之感戴，进退靡安，敢事虚辞，仰违明诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242931_comment'></div>窃念臣将天威而远讨，致贼巢之一空，妙策奇谋，悉遵圣训，破坚却敌，咸得士心，臣实何能，辄膺殊赏，既惭过量，复付重权，是诚叨冒以踰勋，非谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242931", 1242931, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>谦辞</span>而避宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242931_comment'></div>况九江乃控扼之重地，连武昌为襟带之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242931", 1242931, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>要冲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242931_comment'></div>用得其人，周瑜所以败曹公于赤壁，御失其策，隋何所以取黥布于湓江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242931_comment'></div>难使非才，滥膺此寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242931_comment'></div>伏望吝此咽喉之付，以属大臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242931_comment'></div>俯从蝼蚁之诚，使安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242931_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，乞赐寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242931_comment'></div>干冒天威，死有馀罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242931_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1242931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_1242932'>镇南军承宣使、神武副军都统制、江南西路沿江制置使臣岳飞状奏：臣今月十七日准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，除臣男云保义郎、閤门祗候者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242932_comment'></div>伏念臣寒陋无堪，上感圣恩，备员军事，未有涓埃之力，以报国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242932_comment'></div>况臣男云俾从戎伍，未立寸效，岂足仰副异眷，实不遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242932_comment'></div>伏望特赐寝罢，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242932_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript:
