ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月24日</a>　为江南西路舒蕲州制置使，置司江州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月24日</a>　申论虔州平盗将士功赏。作品：《虔贼捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虔贼捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243066")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243066'>镇南军承宣使、神武副军都统制、江南西路舒蕲州制置使岳飞状申：准枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，令飞躬亲前去虔州，讨捕盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243066_comment'></div>飞恭依指挥，起离到吉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243066_comment'></div>有彭大名友等作过，飞先差人招安，不肯听从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243066_comment'></div>分布军马，与贼斗敌，杀死贼徒不知其数，捉到彭铁大并以次首领李动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243066_comment'></div>又往虔州，分遣统领官说谕诸寨头首，不肯听从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243066_comment'></div>遂行进兵，于兴国县衣锦乡一带，节次逢贼见阵，大获胜捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243066_comment'></div>并攻破山寨数百馀座，生擒贼首王彦、钟超、吕添、罗闲十、陈颙、蓝细禾、谢敌、钟大牙、刘八大五、卢高，处置讫，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1243066", 1243066, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>委是</span>尽静，别无未获贼徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243066_comment'></div>今依指挥，将实有功将士，开具等第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243066_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会施行，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1243066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月29日</a>　诏神武副军统制江西制置使岳飞所部，改称神武后军，以飞为统制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年9月29日</a>　再论虔州平盗将士功赏。作品：《再论虔州平盗赏申省札子》<div id='poem_1243039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论虔州平盗赏申省劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年9月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243039")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243039'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、充江南西路舒蕲州制置使岳飞劄子：契勘今年讨捕虔、吉州界盗贼，山寨计数百馀座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243039_comment'></div>其吉盗如彭铁大、李动天两寨，结连肆毒，其徒多至数万，侵犯江西、湖南，及以次首领号为十大王，桀黠为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243039_comment'></div>虔盗如陈颙、罗闲十等四百馀党，自为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243039", 1243039, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>头首</span>，各成寨栅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243039_comment'></div>其徒十馀万众，结为表里，拒敌官军，尤为猖獗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243039_comment'></div>恃赖山险，侵犯数路，广东则循、梅、潮、惠、英、韶、南雄，以至广州，江西则虔州、南安之雩都，江东则建昌军，福建则汀州、邵武等，皆为所攻劫，纵横往来者数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243039_comment'></div>飞顷奉圣旨，提兵讨之，虽正当盛夏，炎瘴交侵，而一时将士奋不顾身，争先用命，以获平荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243039_comment'></div>首领虽众，并就生擒，一无遗类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243039_comment'></div>向非赏罚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1243039", 1243039, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>明均</span>，何以使人尽力如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243039_comment'></div>伏望朝廷特赐详酌，将今来功赏，依去年韩开府收捉福建范汝为恩例施行，庶使有以激劝兵将，缓急可以倚仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243039_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243039_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1243039'>〔小贴子〕契勘飞近蒙朝廷褒擢，飞累具辞免，不蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243039_comment'></div>即非欲夸大微劳，以谋身计，盖恐朝廷将来别有使唤，庶得将士尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243039_comment'></div>区区之愚，毕尽于此，伏乞钧慈特赐详察。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243022'>不可与和，缘虏人羊犬之性，国事隙深，何日可忘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243022_comment'></div>臣乞整兵复三京陵寝，事毕，然后谋河朔，复取旧疆，臣之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243022_comment'></div>臣受陛下深恩厚禄，无一时敢忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1243022_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>诣资善堂见建国公瑷。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>填词抒发退闲之意并暗指和议非计。作品：《小重山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（郭注云“九月，还屯襄阳，填写了《小重山》词”，然岳飞于本年九十月间在鄂州，故此处有误。另据词中“旧山松竹老，阻归程”推知，当作于自临安未返程之前，姑系于此。）</span><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242981_comment'></div>臣窃以御带之职，至近冕旒，非有干城之才，可以任腹心之寄者，不足以当其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242981_comment'></div>臣男云年少惷愚，殊未练达世务，一旦骤迁此职，实非<span class='link' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242982'>少保、枢密副使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣近蒙指挥，依宰臣例，支赐银、绢各一千匹两，臣已两具劄子奏，乞赐蠲免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242982_comment'></div>今月十二日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242982_comment'></div>窃缘臣聚集<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242982", 1242982, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>口累</span>，不至重大，逐月请俸，赡养有馀，若更叨冒锡予，至于无厌，则不知足之患，深可为戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242982_comment'></div>臣不免再具诚恳，仰渎圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242982_comment'></div>伏望睿慈俯垂天鉴，特赐蠲免施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242982_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1242982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月16日</a>　为万俟卨诬劾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月</a>　自楚州还朝，奏乞罢枢密副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月</a>　再上章乞罢枢密副使。作品：《乞解枢柄第二札子》<div id='poem_1242983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞解枢柄第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242983")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242983'>少保、枢密副使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣已具劄子，乞解罢枢密副使职事，至今累日，未蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242983_comment'></div>窃念臣性识<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242983", 1242983, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>疏闇</span>，昧于事机，立功无毫发之微，论罪有丘山之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242983_comment'></div>加以望轻任重，德薄宠殊，荷圣眷之兼容，在孤忠而益畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242983_comment'></div>烦言沓至，私义奚安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242983_comment'></div>欲免累于明恩，理合图于亟去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242983_comment'></div>伏望睿慈察危情之难处，施天造之曲成，听还印于枢庭，许投身于散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242983_comment'></div>欲乞检会臣前奏，早降处分施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242983_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月</a>　第三次上章乞罢枢密副使。作品：《乞解枢柄第三札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（姑系于本月。）</span><div id='poem_1242984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞解枢柄第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242984")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242984'>少保、枢密副使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣已累具劄子，乞解罢枢密副使职事，伏蒙圣恩降诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242984_comment'></div>露章待罪，自惊宠数之过优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242984_comment'></div>温诏示恩，犹閟俞音之下逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242984_comment'></div>再陈愚恳，仰渎渊聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242984_comment'></div>伏念臣滥厕枢庭，误陪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242984", 1242984, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>国论</span>，贪荣滋甚，补报<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242984", 1242984, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>蔑然</span>，岂惟旷职之可虞，抑亦妨贤之是惧，冀保全于终始，宜远引于山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242984_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察其诚心，实非矫饰，速降睿旨，许罢机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242984_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年8月9日</a>　罢枢密副使，充万寿观使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年8月14日</a>　再上章辞两镇节度使充万寿观使。作品：《辞除两镇在京宫观第二札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《辞除两镇在京宫观第一札子》已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞除两镇在京宫观第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年8月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242985")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242985'>少保臣岳飞劄子奏：臣今月十二日伏蒙圣恩，赐臣少保、武胜定国军节度使、充万寿观使告一轴，仍奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242985_comment'></div>臣已谢恩外，缘臣见具劄子辞免，已将告命寄纳临安府，今月十四日伏奉诏命，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242985_comment'></div>窃以两镇节旄，国朝盛典，非有大勋，岂容轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242985_comment'></div>臣前此叨据，常惧弗称，自惟智术短浅，坐糜岁月，考其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242985", 1242985, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>绩用</span>，初无丝毫，安可更尔冒荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242985_comment'></div>矧内祠之任，得侍清光，朝廷所以贵老尊尊，用昭异数，在臣愚分，非所宜处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242985_comment'></div>顾待遇之愈隆，夙夜以思，虽粉身碎骨，何以图报万一，愧深汗溢，感极涕横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242985_comment'></div>重念臣才疏德薄，人微望轻，若不自列，滥当优宠，必致颠隮，上辜宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242985_comment'></div>欲望圣慈追寝成命，除臣一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242985_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年8月14日</a>　僚属散去，军中钱物被拘收。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年10月13日</a>　父子俱下大理寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年12月29日</a>　诏赐死于大理寺。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
武汉（江夏）

id='poem_title_1243041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>措置襄汉乞兵申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243041")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243041'>镇南军承宣使，神武后军统制，江南西路、舒、蕲州、兼荆南、鄂、岳、黄、复州、汉阳军、德安府制置使岳飞状申：恭奉圣旨，恢复襄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243041_comment'></div>仰遵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243041", 1243041, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>庙谟</span>，今已克平五郡，惟信阳未下，已调发军马收复，可以旦夕成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243041_comment'></div>累准御前处分，令飞条具利害防守之策来上，飞已具管见奏闻去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243041_comment'></div>今月初七日再奉指挥，飞之所陈，皆蒙俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243041_comment'></div>然今防守之策，正在乎分屯劲兵，控扼要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243041_comment'></div>飞虽已据数量差军马，于逐处屯驻，然其势力<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1243041", 1243041, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>单寡</span>，难以善后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243041_comment'></div>况今已近九月，天气向寒，边面尤当严备，比闻谍探，虏意犹不可测，飞朝夕计虑，不敢少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243041_comment'></div>且以初者恢复之时，贼徒固守，倍费攻取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243041_comment'></div>继又金贼刘合孛堇、伪齐李成合陕西、河北番、伪之兵，多至数万，并屯邓州，力拒官军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243041_comment'></div>仰赖君相之祐，成此薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243041_comment'></div>今既得之，实控上流，国势所资，尤宜谨守，不可失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243041_comment'></div>飞所乞六万之兵，虽蒙朝廷俞允，然必待杨么贼平，然后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1243041", 1243041, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>抽摘</span>，第恐水势未减，江湖浩涨，杨么未可措手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243041_comment'></div>纵待十二月与正月间，湖水减落，便能平治边面，备御已失机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243041_comment'></div>飞今见管军马，兼拨到牛皋、董先两项，共一千馀人，合飞本军都计二万八千六百一十八人，辎重、火头占破在内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243041_comment'></div>欲望详酌，令湖南留韩京、郝晸两军在潭州弹压外，将任士安、吴锡军马尽数起发，及江西军马内令选择成头项者，勾拨三千人，湖北帅司崔邦弼、颜孝恭并拨付飞，相度分守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243041_comment'></div>计此五项，止是二万人，内有不堪披带辎重、火头之数，不下三、五千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243041_comment'></div>馀乞朝廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1243041", 1243041, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>摘那</span>，以足六万之数，速赐遣发前来，布列诸郡，以为久安之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243041_comment'></div>利害至重，恐不宜缓，伏望早降指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243041_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243041_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1243041'>〔小贴子〕飞被命于鄂州歇泊，别听指挥，谨已遵依外，契勘兵将暴露日久，例皆赤露，天气向寒，衣装未备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243041_comment'></div>欲望速降指挥，令飞本军老小于一处驻劄施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>上疏乞赴行在，奏禀边防。作品：《乞赴行在奏禀边防奏》<div id='poem_1242900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞赴行在奏禀边防奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242900")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242900'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：准枢密院劄子，令臣依已降指挥，前去鄂州歇泊，听候朝廷指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242900_comment'></div>臣除已恭依外，所有臣先条具陈乞事理，未奉指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242900_comment'></div>契勘臣先奉圣训，收复襄阳府等处六州军，除已措置收复随、郢、襄阳、唐、邓了当，只有信阳军，已调发军马前去收复，尅日可下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242900_comment'></div>臣今有边防子细利害，欲量带人从，赴行朝奏禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242900_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，依臣所乞施行。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，32岁</div><div id='143265abb2cc4898b25542a3a9c89aeb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　连续收复邓州、唐州与信阳军，上奏以闻。作品：《复三州奏》<div id='poem_1242988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242988")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242988'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：近准指挥，遣飞进发军马，掩杀番、伪贼马，于五月六日收复随州，七月十七日收复邓州，二十三日收复唐州，并已收复信阳军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242988_comment'></div>并已差官葺治，屯兵防守，已班师江上歇泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242988_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242988_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　复襄阳府等六郡后，奏请先行推赏刘光世军。作品：《乞先推刘光世军掎角赏奏》<div id='poem_1242901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242901' class='poemTitle class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242901")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242901'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：臣先奉圣训，收复襄阳府等处六郡，总率军马，节次见阵，掩杀番、伪贼马，收复州军了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242901_comment'></div>续蒙朝廷令刘光世遣差军马五千人，以为牵制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242901_comment'></div>臣于七月二十三日收复信阳军六郡了毕，光世遣郦琼军马于二十六日到襄阳府臣军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242901_comment'></div>虽其至不及期，然臣之军士知有后援，所以能成薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242901_comment'></div>卒使不沾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242901", 1242901, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>寸赏</span>，恐咈人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242901_comment'></div>伏望圣慈将刘光世所差官兵，特降睿旨，先次推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242901_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　复唐邓信阳军三州后，有奏。作品：《收复唐邓信阳差官奏》<div id='poem_1242902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>知、通</span>等葺治事务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242902_comment'></div>除已开具随、郢州、襄阳府<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242902", 1242902, "Clauses/4/Comments/3")'>知、通</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242902", 1242902, "Clauses/4/Comments/4")'>职次</span>姓名奏闻外，今契勘唐、邓州、信阳军<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242902", 1242902, "Clauses/5/Comments/4")'>知、通</span>、签判<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242902", 1242902, "Clauses/5/Comments/5")'>职次</span>姓名下项，其馀官臣行下逐处安抚司取会，别具奏闻次，今开具下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1242902'>一、唐州二员：修武郎、权知州事高青，借通直郎、权通判单藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242902_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1242902'>一、邓州三员：武翼郎、閤门宣赞舍人、权知州事张应，右承直郎借宣教郎、权通判党尚友，忠训郎借秉义郎、权签判邵俅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242902_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1242902'>一、信阳军二员：承节郎借成忠郎、閤门祗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月</a>　襄汉既平，乞委任重臣经功荆襄。作品：《乞罢制置职事奏》<div id='poem_1242933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢制置职事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242933")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242933'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242933'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：契勘飞昨蒙圣恩，除臣江南西路、舒、蕲州制置使，臣不敢辞免，伏恐朝廷别有使令，实不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242933_comment'></div>方具陈控，继蒙除臣荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使，令臣收复襄阳等六郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242933_comment'></div>臣深体国事之急，愤激于怀，是以承命出征，不暇辞请，今来并已收复<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242933", 1242933, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>了当</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242933_comment'></div>窃念臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242933", 1242933, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>人微望轻</span>，难任斯职，欲望特降睿旨，委任重臣，经画荆、襄，令臣罢制置使职事，依旧充神武后军统制，庶得少安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242933_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月</a>　奏乞侍亲疾。作品：《乞侍亲札子》<div id='poem_1242935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞侍亲疾劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242935")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242935'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣辄具危恳，仰渎睿聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242935_comment'></div>臣愚戆之迹，奋身单微，初无尺寸之先容，独赖圣明之特眷，虽捐躯致命，曾不足以仰酬恩遇之丝毫，思报之心，宁有穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242935_comment'></div>臣近者奉命收复襄汉，去家远涉六月馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242935_comment'></div>臣老母姚氏年几七十，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242935", 1242935, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>侵染</span>疾病，连月未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242935_comment'></div>近复腿脚注痛，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242935", 1242935, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>起止</span>艰难，别无兼侍，以奉汤药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242935_comment'></div>人子之心，实难安处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242935_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣悃愊，无他规避，暂乞许臣在假，以全侍奉之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242935_comment'></div>将本军人马，权暂令统制官王贵、张宪主管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242935_comment'></div>候臣老母稍安，依旧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242935", 1242935, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>管干</span>职事，恭听驱策，结草衔环，誓图报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242935_comment'></div>冒犯雷霆之威，臣无任战惧激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242935_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1242935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月</a>　为清远军节度使湖北路荆潭州制置使。中兴后，诸将建节，未有如飞之年少者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月2日</a>　上章辞建节。作品：《辞建节札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　上《辞建节札子》后未报，又上章。作品：《辞建节第二札子》<div id='poem_1242936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞建节第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242936")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242936'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、充江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣契勘先具辞免江南西路舒蕲等州制置使，蒙恩降诏不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242936_comment'></div>续准省劄，除臣清远军节度使、湖北路荆襄潭州制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242936_comment'></div>臣于今月初二日即具辞免，干犯天聪，至今未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242936_comment'></div>伏念臣谫薄之资，无足比数，误辱圣恩，备员军事，虽竭疲驽，殊无补报，空糜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242936", 1242936, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>饘饩</span>，朝夕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242936", 1242936, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>靡遑</span>，若更贪恋宠荣，不惟取诮人言，亦于臣之冒滥，实所不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242936_comment'></div>伏望睿慈洞察，检会臣前所奏，追寝成命，早降指挥，令臣依旧官资充神武后军统制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242936_comment'></div>庶安愚分，未致颠隮，终图报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242936_comment'></div>紊渎天威，臣无任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242936", 1242936, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>震汗</span>之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242936_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　再上章辞建节。作品：《辞建节第三札子》<div id='poem_1242938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞建节第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242938")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242938'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242938'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、充江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比具辞免清远军节度使，蒙恩降诏不允，遂再沥肝胆之诚，仰渎天听，乞赐追寝成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242938_comment'></div>今月十五日，伏蒙圣恩，再降诏不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242938_comment'></div>臣愚陋无堪，才术凡下，区区武弁，不当辄具汎辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242938", 1242938, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>控免</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242938_comment'></div>惟是旄节之重，实匪所堪，事干国政，不容冒受，惟望早赐追还，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242938_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1242938'><span class='label'>按：</span>《金佗稡编》卷一三，校注本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1242938_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　上章请求追还节度使告命。作品：《缴节度告奏》<div id='poem_1242937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242937' class='poemTitle class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242939'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、充江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣伏准尚书省劄子，以臣辞免清远军节度使，特降圣旨不允，不得再有辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242939_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以不才，幸蒙委使，敢谓涓埃之效，遽叨旄节之荣，若不屡辞，干渎天听，不惟叨冒宠荣，不皇安处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242939_comment'></div>方今戎马侵扰，而误恩若加于人，深虑名器不重，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242939", 1242939, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>劝赏</span>不实，何以厌服公议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242939_comment'></div>臣虽三贡丹诚，宸衷未允，敢望圣慈察臣之愚，实非矫饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242939_comment'></div>所有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242939", 1242939, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>告命</span>，见在鄂州军资库寄纳，伏乞特赐追还，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242939_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1242939_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　诏镇压湖南鼎澧起义军杨太。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　移屯鄂州。襄阳、随、郢、唐、邓、信阳并作襄阳府路隶之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　行营田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　登黄鹤楼北望，填词以明收复中原的决心。作品：《满江红 登黄鹤楼有感》<div id='poem_166926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 id='poem_sentence_0_166926'>遥望中原，荒烟外、许多城郭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166926'>想当年、花遮柳护，凤楼龙阁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166926'>万岁山前珠翠绕，蓬壶殿里笙歌作。<div id='poem_sentence_2_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_166926'>到而今、铁骑满郊畿，风尘恶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166926_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_166926'>兵安在，膏锋锷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_166926'>民安在，填沟壑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_166926'>叹江山如故，千村寥落。<div id='poem_sentence_6_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_166926'>何日请缨提锐旅，一鞭直渡清河洛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_166926'>却归来、再续汉阳游，骑黄鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_166926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242947")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_0_1242947_comment'></div>今月十六日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，依已降诏旨不允，不得再有陈请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242947_comment'></div>伏念臣才术空疏，智识<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242947", 1242947, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>凡下</span>，方恳辞检校少保之恩，岂谓复进招讨之任，荐膺眷渥，抚己惊惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242947_comment'></div>切惟阃外之重，责任非轻，自匪德望服人，韬略迈众，何以仰副陛下遴选委寄之意，如臣不才，曷足当此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242947_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣之衷，实欲少安分守，早赐追还成命，庶协<span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月</a>　上章辞宣抚副使。作品：《辞宣抚副使札子》<div id='poem_1242949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞宣抚副使劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242949")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242949'>检校少保、镇宁崇信军节度使、湖北襄阳府路招讨使兼本路营田使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣三月十八日，准御前金字牌递到枢密院劄子，枢密院奏，勘会岳飞已降指挥，除湖北、京西南路宣抚副使，奉圣旨，疾速兼程前去鄂州，措置军事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242949_comment'></div>臣闻命震惊，罔知所措，臣近叨受招讨使，不容牢辞，又蒙圣恩授以前件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242949_comment'></div>切念臣一介寒贱，误膺器使，顾土宇恢复之迹，未见尺寸，而厚恩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242949", 1242949, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>醲赏</span>，涯分已踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242949_comment'></div>且以宣抚之重名，实寄专征之大事，自非廊庙近臣、勋伐高世者，岂当冒躐而居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242949_comment'></div>异时付托失人，或误驱策，虽粉臣骨，曷足以谢陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242949_comment'></div>兼招讨使权不为不重，若更加以甚高非常之宠，必起<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242949", 1242949, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>负乘斯夺</span>之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242949_comment'></div>所有宣抚副使恩命，实难祗受，伏望追寝误恩，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242949_comment'></div>臣无任悚惧恭听宸命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242949_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月12日</a>　都督府令飞将带精兵，疾去襄阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月26日</a>　母姚氏卒于鄂州军中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月</a>　不俟报，解官而去，扶榇至庐山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='52d43ff582414d259d01ff1bda084998_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("52d43ff582414d259d01ff1bda084998");'><span id='52d43ff582414d259d01ff1bda084998_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月17日</a>　以孤军无援，复还鄂州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月</a>　以目疾申省乞致仕。作品：《乞致仕养疾申省状》<div id='poem_1243059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕养疾申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243059")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243059'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使岳飞状申：□□近巡按边□指挥事宜，缘□□□□□□□收军马于襄阳府等处屯□□□□□□□令致仕养疾，未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243059_comment'></div>九□□□□□□□鄂州，其目疾愈觉昏暗不□□□□□□□假，令参谋官薛弼、参议官□□□□□□□宣抚司事务，今来所苦眼□□□□□□□方此贼马侵扰，主上亲□□□□□□□劳，稍能勉强，岂敢托疾，以□□□□□□□事理，伏望速赐施行，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1243059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年10月</a>　诏提兵东下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年10月</a>　遣医官皇甫知常及僧中印至军疗治目疾，并赐御札劳问，且趣飞军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年10月</a>　受诏前往江州，作诗寄庐山友人慧海。作品：《寄浮图慧海》<span class='inlineComment2'>（王曾瑜将此诗系于绍兴十年岳飞率军北上之时，见《岳飞新传》，中国书籍出版社2016年版，第232页。）</span><div id='poem_166919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄浮图慧海</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_166919")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_166919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166919'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166919'>湓浦庐山几度秋，长江万折向东流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166919'>男儿立志扶王室，圣主专师灭虏酋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166919'>功业要刊燕石上，归休终伴赤松游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_166919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_166919'>丁宁寄语东林老，莲社从此著力修<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上宋岳珂《金佗粹编》卷一九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_166919'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_166919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年10月</a>　奉诏启行，仍以目疾乞解军务。作品：《目疾乞解军务札子》<div id='poem_1242955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>目疾乞解军务劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242955")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242955'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使臣岳飞状奏：臣先为目疾昏痛，不能视物，在假服药医治，累奏乞致仕，将宣抚司事务权令参谋官薛弼、参议官李若虚管干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242955_comment'></div>已申奏朝廷，听候指挥去讫，未蒙回降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242955_comment'></div>十月十五日夜，据参谋官薛弼传到御前劄子一封，付岳飞，系金字牌降到，内系黄纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242955_comment'></div>臣遂拆开，认是宸翰，臣即时遥拜跪领，不觉感激涕泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242955_comment'></div>臣平日切切思报陛下之心，惟冀当此大敌，少展区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242955_comment'></div>适以病目，转觉昏暗，臣私心不胜痛愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242955_comment'></div>又于十六日据薛弼申，累准金字牌降到御封枢密院劄子，催促全军人马前去江、池州，称已勾抽襄阳等处军马前来，犹恐迟缓，已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242955", 1242955, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>整龊</span>在寨军马，止候兜请钱粮，俵散衣赐了当，先次起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242955_comment'></div>臣比在假，每日连并服药，全未见效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242955_comment'></div>伏望睿慈检会臣累奏事理，速赐施行，庶几不误国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242955_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1242955_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5109c770be2045619a3f02a4a786506c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5109c770be2045619a3f02a4a786506c");'><span id='5109c770be2045619a3f02a4a786506c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，34岁</div><div id='5109c770be2045619a3f02a4a786506c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年11月</a>　奉诏还军鄂州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年12月21日</a>　诏赴行在奏事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ace827acb75646a7814b6a2bbe54c9bd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ace827acb75646a7814b6a2bbe54c9bd");'><span id='ace827acb75646a7814b6a2bbe54c9bd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，35岁</div><div id='ace827acb75646a7814b6a2bbe54c9bd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年7月</a>　还镇鄂州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年8月</a>　上章乞以本军进讨刘豫。作品：《乞本军进讨刘豫札子》<div id='poem_1242910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞本军进讨刘豫劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242910")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242910'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242910'>太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：贼豫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242910", 1242910, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>逋诛</span>，尚穴中土，陵寝乏祀，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242910", 1242910, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>皇图</span>偏安，陛下六飞时巡，越在海际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242910_comment'></div>天下之愚夫愚妇莫不疾首痛心，愿得伸锄奋梃，以致死于敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242910_comment'></div>而陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242910", 1242910, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>审重</span>此举，累年于兹，虽尝分命将臣，鼎峙江、汉，而皆仅令自守以待敌，不敢远攻而求胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242910_comment'></div>是以天下忠愤之气，日以沮丧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242910_comment'></div>中原来苏之望，日以衰息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242910_comment'></div>岁月益久，污染渐深，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242910", 1242910, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>趋向</span>一背，不复可以转移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242910_comment'></div>此其利害，诚为易见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242910_comment'></div>臣待罪阃外，不能宣国威灵，克殄小丑，致神州隔于王化，虏、伪穴于宫阙，死有馀罪，敢逃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1242910", 1242910, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>司败</span>之诛！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242910_comment'></div>陛下比者寝閤之命，圣断已坚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242910_comment'></div>咸谓恢复之功，指日可冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242910_comment'></div>何至今日，尚未决策北向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242910_comment'></div>臣愿因此时，上禀成算，不烦济师，只以本军进讨，庶少塞瘝官之咎，以成陛下寤寐中兴之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242910_comment'></div>顺天之道，因民之情，以曲直为壮老，以逆顺为强弱，万全之效，兹焉可必，惟陛下力断而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242910_comment'></div>不胜大愿，区区臣子下情，昧死干冒天威，无任战慄恐惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242910_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1242910_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年8月</a>　上章乞自临安移都上游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月14日</a>　奏乞进屯淮甸，不许。作品：《乞进屯淮甸札子》<div id='poem_1242912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞进屯淮甸劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242912")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242912'>太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣伏睹陛下移跸建康，将遂恢图之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242912_comment'></div>近忽传淮西军马溃叛，郦琼等<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242912", 1242912, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>迫胁</span>军民而去，然事出仓卒，实非士众本心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242912_comment'></div>亦闻半道逃归人数不少，于国计未有所损，不足上轸渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242912_comment'></div>臣度今日事势，彼必未能便有举动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242912_comment'></div>襄阳上流，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242912", 1242912, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>目即</span>亦无贼马侵犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242912_comment'></div>唯是淮甸迫近行在，臣愿提全军进屯，万一番、伪窥伺，臣当竭力奋击，期于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242912", 1242912, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>破灭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242912_comment'></div>仍乞别遣军马，措置襄阳一带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242912_comment'></div>伏乞睿断详酌施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242912_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月22日</a>　上章请以明堂任子恩，官张所子宗本，仍张俊例补文资。作品：《乞以明堂恩奏张所男宗本奏》<div id='poem_1242909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以明堂恩奏张所男宗本奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242909")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242909'>起复太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞状奏：臣窃见张俊例，初除太尉，陈乞奏荐男于文资内安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242909_comment'></div>臣技能蔑取，勋伐无闻，遭际圣明，承乏将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242909_comment'></div>伏念臣昨于建炎初，因上书论事，罪废，偶幸逃死，实出圣造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242909_comment'></div>于时孤孑一身，狼狈羁旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242909_comment'></div>因诣招抚使张所，所一见，与臣言两河、燕云利害，适偶契合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242909_comment'></div>臣自白身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242909", 1242909, "Clauses/19/Comments/1")'>借补</span>修武郎、閤门宣赞舍人，充中军统领，寻又升统制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242909_comment'></div>其后张所军次北京，蒙朝廷贬责南方，卒以节死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242909_comment'></div>臣念靖康以来，奋不顾身，为国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1242909", 1242909, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>捍难</span>者，不为无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242909_comment'></div>而其间误国败事者，固亦不乏，然圣恩宽大，终于一切<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242909", 1242909, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>矜贷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242909_comment'></div>若张所实先意两河，而身未北渡，已遭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1242909", 1242909, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>横议</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242909_comment'></div>今其身名凋丧，后嗣零落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242909_comment'></div>使臣不言，臣则有负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242909_comment'></div>欲望矜怜，将臣今岁奏荐恩例，奏补张所男宗本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242909_comment'></div>依张俊例，于文资内安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242909_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1242909_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2d26284a0d804006baaacfe03171de4e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2d26284a0d804006baaacfe03171de4e");'><span id='2d26284a0d804006baaacfe03171de4e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>，36岁</div><div id='2d26284a0d804006baaacfe03171de4e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年2月13日</a>　诏由江州还军鄂州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年4月7日</a>　条具伐金利害，请早降指挥。作品：《奏审已条具曲折未准指挥札子》<div id='poem_1242913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏审已条具曲折未准指挥劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年4月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242913")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242913'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242913'>太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣自去冬闻金贼废刘豫，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242913", 1242913, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>可乘</span>之机，是以屡贡管见，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242913", 1242913, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>尘渎</span>天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242913_comment'></div>三月二十六日，领枢密院劄子，奉圣旨，令臣条具曲折以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242913_comment'></div>臣喜而不寐，以谓陛下慨然英断，将欲兴王师，举大事，以雪积年之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242913_comment'></div>故臣辄忘浅陋，周述利害，仰紊睿明，觊或采纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242913_comment'></div>今月初七日，臣所差人回，未蒙朝廷处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242913_comment'></div>伏望早降指挥，俯赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242913_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年2月</a>　第三次上章辞开府。作品：《辞开府第三札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《辞开府第二札子》已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞开府第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242964")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242964'>太尉、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣契勘已具辞免除臣开府仪同三司，加食邑五百户、食实封三百户恩命，今月二十七日，蒙降到诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242964_comment'></div>臣近者累犯天威，力辞恩宠，庶几陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242964", 1242964, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>洞烛</span>危恳，终赐矜从，而温诏谆谆，未回睿听，跼地吁天，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242964_comment'></div>夫爵赏者，人君所以为厉世磨钝之具，人臣得之，所以荣耀乡里，而显贲宗族也，谁不欲贪多而务得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242964_comment'></div>然得所当得，固以为荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242964_comment'></div>受所非受，反足为辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242964_comment'></div>伏念臣奋迹羁单，被恩优腆，使臣终身只守此官，已踰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242964", 1242964, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>涯量</span>，岂可分外更冒显荣，遂速颠隮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242964_comment'></div>虽陛下推天地至宽之量，在所兼容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242964_comment'></div>而微臣抱金石图报之心，宁无自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242964_comment'></div>所有臣为将不效，献言悖理之实，臣于累奏中固已缕陈，更不敢谆复，紊烦圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242964_comment'></div>伏望陛下检会臣累次劄子，追寝成命，特降俞音，庶使微臣少安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242964_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1242964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月</a>　第四次上章辞开府。作品：《辞开府第四札子》<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年4月</a>　上章乞同宋使往谒陵寝，并观敌衅。作品：《论虏情奏略》《奏审谒陵寝行期札子》<div id='poem_1242916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论虏情奏略<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1242916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242916'>北虏自靖康以来，以和款我者十馀年矣，不悟其奸，受祸至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242916_comment'></div>今复无事请和，此殆必有肘腋之虞，未能攻犯边境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242916_comment'></div>又刘豫初废，藩篱空虚，故诡为此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242916_comment'></div>名以地归我，然实寄之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242916_comment'></div>臣请量带轻骑，随二使祗谒陵寝，因以往观敌衅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242916_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1242917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242917?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_1242917_comment'></div>臣见办集行役，只候得士袅、张焘关报行期，便同起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242917_comment'></div>或恐陛下别有使令，愿赐一一训敕。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年6月3日</a>　复河南故地，上章乞免荆湖北路、京西路便宜辟置官员。作品：《乞免便宜辟置札子》<div id='poem_1242914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免便宜辟置劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年6月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞解军务第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242966")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242966'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣顷以多病易衰，仰渎宸听，乞退处丘垄，以便养痾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242966_comment'></div>伏蒙陛下未忍弃去，尚閟俞音，不免<span class='link' "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>邀君</span>之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242966_comment'></div>今讲好已定，两宫天眷不日可还，偃武休兵，可期岁月，臣之所请，无避事之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242966_comment'></div>臣不揆庸愚，幸免此二事，止以疾病馀生，恐误任使，久享厚禄，坐费太仓，蚤夜以思，身不遑处，所以不避鈇钺，至于再而不自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242966_comment'></div>伏望陛下垂博照之明，回盖高之听，曲加仁恻，洞照愚衷，使一夫之微，终遂其欲，特许退休，就营医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242966_comment'></div>臣不胜感戴圣德愿望之至。<div class='inline' href='/Writing/1242968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞男云特转恩命第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1242968_comment'></div>伏念臣遭遇宸眷，倍于常伦，初无显赫之功，以称褒崇之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242968_comment'></div>又况臣男云愚惷无知，涓埃未效，叠蒙优渥，以臣之故，冒滥爵禄，已为过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242968_comment'></div>今若又宠以异数，使之叨据，不唯使云不知名器之重，或就<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242968", 1242968, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>骄溢</span>，上则负陛下之恩，下则取缙绅之谤，并臣之罪，亦复难逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242968_comment'></div>伏望圣慈俯回天听，特赐追寝，实为臣父子之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242968_comment'></div>臣不胜激切震汗之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242968_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月12日</a>　再上章乞请优加褒异张所，以劝天下忠义之士。作品：《再乞褒赠张所申省札子》<div id='poem_1243053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞褒赠张所申省劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243053")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243053'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使岳飞劄子：飞窃闻好生恶死，天下常情，若临大难而不变，视死如归，则非忠义之士，有所不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243053_comment'></div>伏见左通直郎、直龙图阁张所以忠许国，义不顾身，虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243053", 1243053, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>斧钺</span>在前，凛然不易其色，终能以全节自守而不屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243053_comment'></div>不惟飞知之，士大夫无不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243053_comment'></div>今蒙朝廷已叙复元官，恩至渥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243053_comment'></div>然区区之心欲望更赐敷奏，特与优加褒异，庶使天下忠义之士，皆知所劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243053_comment'></div>冒渎钧严，飞不胜皇惧待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1243053_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月</a>　第三次上章辞子云转武显大夫遥郡刺史。作品：《辞男云特转恩命第三札子》<div id='poem_1242969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞男云特转恩命第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242969")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242969'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣近两具辞免臣男云武显大夫、遥郡刺史，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，依已降指挥，不允，不得再有陈请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242969_comment'></div>恭读之际，愧汗交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242969_comment'></div>伏念臣叨荷圣恩，实倍伦等，曲折之辞，前已备述，不敢喋喋，上渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242969_comment'></div>臣以辞免开府恩命，重蒙玉音戒谕丁宁，又不敢固违天意，跼蹐拜命，已切悚惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242969_comment'></div>今若并臣男云无功进职，是臣辞荣而益荣，避禄而邀禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242969_comment'></div>恩虽至厚，公议谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242969_comment'></div>伏望特简渊衷，俯回洞照，特赐寝免，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242969_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月</a>　第四次上章辞子云转武显大夫遥郡刺史。作品：《辞男云特转恩命第四札子》<div id='poem_1242970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞男云特转恩命第四劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242970")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242970'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣先三具劄子，辞免臣男云武显大夫、遥郡刺史恩命事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242970_comment'></div>今月二十一日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，依已降指挥，不允，不得再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242970_comment'></div>臣闻正己然后可以正物，自治然后可以治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242970_comment'></div>臣奋身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242970", 1242970, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>疏逖</span>，冒国宠荣，陛下误恩，擢置重任，以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242970", 1242970, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>孱陋</span>之资，将军旅之众，顾惟匪称，夙夜惶惧，惟恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242970", 1242970, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>检饬</span>修省，有所未至，不足以服众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242970_comment'></div>比者男云未尝立功，遽迁优秩，在臣私分，实不皇处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242970_comment'></div>臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242970", 1242970, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>庸懦</span>无能，方将勉竭驽钝，仰图报称，而自使其子受无功之赏，则是臣不能正己而自治，将何以率人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242970_comment'></div>伏望陛下怜臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242970", 1242970, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>拙直</span>，察臣愚衷，早赐俞音，收还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242970_comment'></div>容臣男他日大立战功，然后命之以官，亦未为晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242970_comment'></div>所有官告一轴，除已令本司签厅牒鄂州，于军资库寄纳外，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242970_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　适斋反对和议被谪，死贬所。作诗哀悼适斋先生，表彰其功德。作品：《诔适斋先生》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年1月</a>　为高宗所赐《诸葛亮等屯田三事》作跋，明恢复之志。作品：《御书屯田三事跋》<div id='poem_1243087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书屯田三事跋<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243087")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243087'>臣闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>先正</span>司马光有言：「德胜才谓之君子，才胜德谓之小人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243087_comment'></div>论人者能审于才德之分，则无失人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243087_comment'></div>曹操募百姓，屯田许下，所在积粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243087_comment'></div>诸葛亮分兵屯田，而百姓安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243087_comment'></div>羊祜怀远近，得江、汉之心，亦以垦田获利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243087_comment'></div>若三子者，知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>重本</span>务农，使兵无艰食，其谋猷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>术略</span>，皆不在人下，才有足称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243087_comment'></div>然操酷虐变诈，揽申、商之法术，虽号超世之杰，岂正直中和者所为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243087_comment'></div>许劭谓清平之奸贼，乱世之英雄，其德有贬云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243087_comment'></div>亮开诚心，布公道，邦域之内，畏而爱之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243087_comment'></div>祜增修德信，以怀柔初附，则德过于操远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243087_comment'></div>观亮素志，欲龙骧虎视，包括四海，以兴汉室，天不假以年，遽有渭南之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243087_comment'></div>祜辅晋武，慨然有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>并吞</span>之心，后平吴，身不及见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243087_comment'></div>二子有意于功名，而志弗克伸，惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243087_comment'></div>臣庸德薄才，诚不敢妄论古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243087_comment'></div>伏蒙陛下亲洒宸翰，铺述二三子屯田足食之事，俯以赐臣，臣敢不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>策驽砺钝</span>，仰副圣意万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243087_comment'></div>夫服田力穑，乃亦有秋，农夫职尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243087_comment'></div>用屯田以足兵食，诚不为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243087_comment'></div>臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1243087", 1243087, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>不揆</span>，愿迟之岁月，敢以奉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243087_comment'></div>要使忠信以进德，不为君子之弃，则臣将勉其所不逮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243087_comment'></div>若夫鞭挞四夷，尊强中国，扶宗社于再安，辅明天子，以享万世无疆之休，臣窃有区区之志，不知得伸欤否也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243087_comment'></div>绍兴十年正月初一日，武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、武昌郡开国公、食邑四千户、食实封一千七百户臣岳飞谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1243087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　遣李宝等与金人战。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　为恢复计，上章乞定储嗣。作品：《乞定储嗣奏略》<div id='poem_1242920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞定储嗣奏略<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242920")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242920'>今欲恢复，必先正国本，以安人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242920_comment'></div>然后陛下不常厥居，以示不忘复雠之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1242920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月1日</a>　授少保兼河南府路陕西河东河北路招讨使，加食邑食封。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月2日</a>　李宝等杀死鹘旋郎郡，复败金人于黄河南岸，作申省状。作品：《鹘旋郎君捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹘旋郎君捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243070")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243070'>少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使岳飞状申：据本司统领官李宝、孙彦申：「探得金贼四太子前军四个千户，将领马军大队四千馀骑，前来宛亭县界荆冈下寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243070_comment'></div>宝等于五月二十四日晚，部领人船前去，一更以来，劫杀金贼大寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243070_comment'></div>杀死并<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243070", 1243070, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>拥掩</span>入黄河，不知数目，杀死千户三人并鹘旋郎君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243070_comment'></div>夺到白旗一面，上写都元帅越国王前军四千户字，夺到马一千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243070_comment'></div>六月二日，有番贼金牌郎君会起东京以北番贼大队前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243070_comment'></div>宝等统率人兵，向前掩杀，贼兵败走，望南逃遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243070_comment'></div>追杀二十馀里，杀死、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1243070", 1243070, "Clauses/22/Comments/1")'>拥掩</span>入黄河，不知其数，夺到器甲不少，委是大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243070_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243070_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　改河南北诸路招讨使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　赐札趣援刘锜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　第三次上章辞少保。作品：《辞少保第三札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《辞少保札子》《辞少保第二札子》俱佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞少保第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242971")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242971'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242971'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣伏蒙圣恩，除臣少保，加食邑七百户、食实封三百户，臣已两具辞免，今月初十日，伏奉诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242971_comment'></div>臣闻忠臣之事君，计功而受赏，量力而受官，不为苟得，以贪爵禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242971_comment'></div>况师旅方兴，事功未著，臣方同士卒之甘苦，明将佐以恩威，冀成尺寸之功，仰报君父之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242971_comment'></div>岂可身被厚宠，而恝然不以当锋刃、冒矢石者为心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242971_comment'></div>所有少保恩命，臣实不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242971_comment'></div>伏望陛下日月照临，乾坤覆载，察臣肺腑，追寝异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242971_comment'></div>臣愿凭陛下雷霆之威，托宗庙山岳之福，罄竭驽钝，期效涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242971_comment'></div>候将来功绩有成，臣将拜手稽首，祗承休命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242971_comment'></div>诚恳迫切，至于再三，干冒天威，臣不任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242971", 1242971, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>战悸</span>恐惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242971_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1242971_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月19日</a>　第四次上章辞少保。作品：《辞少保第四札子》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cdb78f1e87f643aa935563a68719f9f0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdb78f1e87f643aa935563a68719f9f0");'><span id='cdb78f1e87f643aa935563a68719f9f0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='cdb78f1e87f643aa935563a68719f9f0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年8月</a>　金人犯淮阳府，遣兵救之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年8月30日</a>　第五次上章辞少保。作品：《辞少保第五札子》<div id='poem_1242973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242973?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞少保第五劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年8月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242973")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242973_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242973'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242973'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣伏蒙圣恩，特降告命，除臣少保，加食邑七百户、食实封三百户，臣已四具劄子辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242973_comment'></div>八月三十日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，不允，令日下祗受，仍依累降诏旨，不得再有陈请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242973_comment'></div>臣之事君，义无有己，若夫贪慕爵禄，务荣一身，而不以国家为念，则非臣之所忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242973_comment'></div>比者羯胡败盟，再犯河南之地，肆为残忍，人神共愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242973_comment'></div>臣方将策驽砺钝，冀效尺寸，以报陛下天地生成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242973_comment'></div>今则虏骑寇边，未见殄灭，区区之志，未效一二，臣复以身为谋，惟贪爵禄，则诚恐不足为将士之劝，而报恩无所，万诛何赎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242973_comment'></div>伏望睿慈追寝成命，特赐俞音，姑诏有司，留以为臣异时涓埃之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242973_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242973_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年9月1日</a>　召赴行在。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8b33b87bb0ca44dcbd78a9a62e3f8ee0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8b33b87bb0ca44dcbd78a9a62e3f8ee0");'><span id='8b33b87bb0ca44dcbd78a9a62e3f8ee0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1141')">1140-1141年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='8b33b87bb0ca44dcbd78a9a62e3f8ee0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年10月</a>　川陕告急。命王贵、董先援之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年11月</a>　命益光州兵援田邦直。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年1月</a>　宗弼再南寇。奏乞会诸帅破敌。作品：《乞会诸帅兵破敌奏》<div id='poem_1242925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞会诸帅兵破敌奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242925")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242925'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242925'>少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：近据探报，虏酋将自寿春等处入寇淮西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242925_comment'></div>臣契勘目即上流未有贼马侵犯，欲乞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242925", 1242925, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>圣慈</span>令臣提军前去，会合诸帅，同共掩击，兵力既合，必成大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242925_comment'></div>伏望速赐指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242925_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年1月</a>　赐御札令进兵江州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月4日</a>　上章献长驱京洛，取金巢穴之策。作品：《乞出京洛奏略》<div id='poem_1242927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出京洛奏略<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1242927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242927'>契勘虏既举国来寇，巢穴必虚，若长驱京、洛，虏必奔命，可以坐制其弊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1242927_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1242927'><span class='label'>按：</span>《金佗稡编》卷一二，校注本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1242927_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月4日</a>　上章欲亲至蕲黄，相度形势利害以退金兵。作品：《乞出蕲黄奏略》<div id='poem_1242928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出蕲黄奏略<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月4日）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_1242928'>今虏犯淮西，臣若捣虚，势必得利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242928_comment'></div>万一以为寇方在近，未暇远图，乞且亲至蕲、黄，相度形势利害，以议攻却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242928_comment'></div>且虏知荆、鄂宿师，必自九江进援，今若出此，贵得不拘，使敌罔测。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1242928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1242928'><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月9日</a>　始奉出兵江州之诏，下令以十一日就道，且以奏闻。<br /></div>
-----end
