-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8978eba9e4164470aa1ba10887e02f5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8978eba9e4164470aa1ba10887e02f5e");'><span id='8978eba9e4164470aa1ba10887e02f5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，32岁</div><div id='8978eba9e4164470aa1ba10887e02f5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月17日</a>　复襄阳府。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1fa6a35a26ae4a8e8aec26798e7988e1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fa6a35a26ae4a8e8aec26798e7988e1");'><span id='1fa6a35a26ae4a8e8aec26798e7988e1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，32岁</div><div id='1fa6a35a26ae4a8e8aec26798e7988e1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　奏画守襄阳等郡及措置营田事。作品：《画守襄阳等郡札子》<div id='poem_1242898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画守襄阳等郡劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242898")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242898'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣六月二十三日酉时，准御前金字牌，伏蒙圣慈特降亲札处分，令臣条具襄阳、随、郢利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242898_comment'></div>臣窃观金贼、刘豫皆有可取之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242898_comment'></div>金贼累年之间，贪婪横逆，无所不至，今所爱惟金帛、子女，志已骄堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242898_comment'></div>刘豫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>僭臣</span>贼子，虽以俭约结民，而人心终不忘宋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242898_comment'></div>攻讨之谋，正不宜缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242898_comment'></div>苟岁月迁延，使得修治<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>城壁</span>，添兵聚粮，而后取之，必倍费力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242898_comment'></div>陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>渊谋远略</span>，非臣所知，以臣自料，如及此时，以精兵二十万直捣中原，恢复故疆，民心效顺，诚易为力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242898_comment'></div>此则国家长久之策也，在陛下睿断耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242898_comment'></div>若姑以目前论之，襄阳、随、郢地皆膏腴，民力不支，苟行营田之法，其利为厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242898_comment'></div>然即今将已七月，未能耕垦，来年入春，即可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>措画</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242898_comment'></div>陛下欲驻大兵于鄂州，则襄阳、随、郢量留军马，又于安、复、汉阳亦量驻兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242898_comment'></div>兵势相援，漕运相继，荆门、荆南声援亦已相接，江、淮、荆湖皆可奠安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242898_comment'></div>六州之屯，且以正兵六万，为固守之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242898_comment'></div>就拨江西、湖南粮斛，朝廷支降券钱，为一年<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1242898", 1242898, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>支遣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242898_comment'></div>候营田就绪，军储既成，则朝廷无馈饷之忧，进攻退守，皆兼利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242898_comment'></div>惟是葺治之初，未免艰难，必仰朝廷微有以资之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242898_comment'></div>基本既立，后之利源无有穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242898_comment'></div>又此地夏秋则江水涨隔，外可以御寇，内足以运粮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242898_comment'></div>至冬后春初，江水浅涩，吾资粮已备，可以坐待矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242898_comment'></div>于今所先，在乎速备粮食，斟量屯守之兵，可善其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242898_comment'></div>臣识闇不学，辄具管见，仰报圣问，辞拙事直，伏乞圣慈裁决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1242898_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣不胜屏营战慄之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1242898_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1242898_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1242898'>〔贴黄〕臣见今只候粮食稍足，即便过江北，虽番、伪贼马势重，臣定竭力剿戮，不敢少负陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1242898_comment'></div>伏乞特宽宵旰之念，不胜庆幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1242898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　遣牛皋复随州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　上疏条具襄阳随郢三郡防守。作品：《条具荆襄相度移治及差官奏》<div id='poem_1242899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条具荆襄相度移治及差官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242899")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242899'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：臣于六月二十八日，准御前金字牌递到枢密院六月十六日劄子，备奉圣旨，令臣条具收复襄阳、随、郢三郡防守，相度移治山寨等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242899_comment'></div>今条具画一，开具下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1242899'>一、臣收复到襄阳、随、郢三州，即时逐急权行差官，葺治州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242899_comment'></div>实以此三州止有空城，公吏、军民自缘久罹兵火，或被驱虏，或遭杀戮，甚为荒残，全藉有心力官抚绥葺治，招诱人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242899_comment'></div>所有襄阳府，已差武功大夫、本军干办官张旦借左武大夫、权唐邓郢州襄阳府安抚使、兼知襄阳军府事，亲卫大夫、安州观察使牛皋权唐邓郢州襄阳府安抚副使，武义大夫、荣州团练使李道充唐邓郢州襄阳府四州都统制，承信郎、本军准备差遣孙革借右承务郎、权签书襄阳府判官厅公事讫，今来葺治渐成次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242899_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1242899'>一、郢州已差承节郎、本军准备差遣周识借右承奉郎、权知郢州，右迪功郎、本军准备差遣李旦借承奉郎、权本州通判讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242899_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1242899'>一、随州已差右将仕郎、本军准备差遣孙翚借承奉郎、权知随州，下州文学蒋庭俊借右修职郎、权本州节度推官讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242899_comment'></div>近访闻逐州官葺治渐成次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242899_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1242899'>一、臣所奏差官等事理，更合取自指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242899_comment'></div>如蒙俞允，乞降差劄施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242899_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1242899'>一、臣蒙朝廷支拨粮三十三万硕，水脚钱一十七万贯，委沈昭远等催督应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242899_comment'></div>今来臣自至襄阳已及月馀，止有粮五千七百馀硕至军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242899_comment'></div>伏望特降睿旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242899_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1242899'>右画一开具在前，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1242899_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='860133fb0588493eb694bdae253dd4a4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("860133fb0588493eb694bdae253dd4a4");'><span id='860133fb0588493eb694bdae253dd4a4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，34岁</div><div id='860133fb0588493eb694bdae253dd4a4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月18日</a>　自九江进屯襄阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月24日</a>　乞便宜处置蠹政害民、赃污不法之吏。作品：《乞便宜黜赃吏申省札子》<div id='poem_1243048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞便宜黜赃吏申省劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年6月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243048")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243048'>检校少保、镇宁崇信军节度使、充湖北京西路招讨使兼本路营田使岳飞劄子：飞一介寒微，误蒙朝廷委寄两路，不敢不竭愚钝，以图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243048_comment'></div>契勘管下州县例经残破，正赖抚绥，切虑州县官或有蠹政害民、赃污不法之人，当此安集之初，易以搔扰，若不稍加振厉，则民户难以安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243048_comment'></div>欲望特降指挥，如有似此之人，许本司一面对移，事理重者放罢，仍具<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243048", 1243048, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>情犯</span>职名奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243048_comment'></div>所贵官吏修举职事，不敢苟简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243048_comment'></div>伏候钧旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月</a>　李通首倡归顺，上章奏闻。作品：《李通归顺奏》<div id='poem_1242907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李通归顺奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242907")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242907'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242907'>检校少保、镇宁崇信军节度使、充湖北襄阳府路招讨使兼本路营田使臣岳飞状奏：契勘臣尝以国难未除，虏祸方炽，窃有意于恢复之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242907_comment'></div>深筹逆计，以为中原之士，性具五常，岂无忠义思报国家，特以身陷虏、伪之郊，未能奋发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242907_comment'></div>于是多遣信实之人密行，宣布朝廷之德意，说谕约结，俾其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242907", 1242907, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>磨濯</span>一心，以待王师之举，相为应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242907_comment'></div>今有虢州栾川知县、修武郎李通将带五百馀人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242907", 1242907, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>首倡</span>归顺，已到邓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242907_comment'></div>除已差官前去引接、犒劳外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242907_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年7月2日</a>　命移文伪境，于宣抚职位中增“河东”及“节制河北路”。申都督府辞免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年7月</a>　上章乞寝罢阶内添入河东及节制河北路字。作品：《乞免带河东宣抚申都督府状》<div id='poem_1243058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免带河东宣抚申都督府状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243058")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243058'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼本路营田使岳飞状申：准都督行府劄子：「勘会行府恭被圣训，应措置军事，一面相度施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243058_comment'></div>契勘岳少保已除湖北京西路宣抚副使，所有将来进发至京西路分行下伪界文字，合添入『河东』二字，以『湖北京西河东宣抚副使』系阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243058_comment'></div>其行移湖北以里州军，及关申朝廷并行府等文字，自合依旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243058_comment'></div>已于三月三十日劄下岳少保照会施行去讫，须议指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243058_comment'></div>右勘会若将来有河北申到本司军前文字，即听行节制，仍于阶内添入『节制河北路』五字，馀依已劄下事理施行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243058_comment'></div>除已遵依指挥施行外，契勘河东、河北两路，近除有梁兴等前来之后外，别无前来之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243058_comment'></div>所有前项所准指挥，令飞阶内添入「河东」及「节制河北路」字，伏乞行府特赐指挥寝罢施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243058_comment'></div>伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年8月</a>　遣杨再兴复长水县，上章奏捷。作品：《复西京长水县捷奏》<div id='poem_1242990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复西京长水县捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242990'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使臣岳飞状奏：据统制官王贵申：「遵依指挥，差武经郎、第四副将杨再兴等统率军马，前去收复西京长水县去后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242990_comment'></div>今据申：八月十三日进兵到长水县界业阳，逢伪齐顺州安抚张宣赞下孙都统，并后军统制满在，拥贼兵数千人拒敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242990_comment'></div>当时分布军马，掩击贼众，杀死五百馀人，生擒后军统制满在并徒众一百馀人，及当阵杀获孙都统首级，其馀残党尽皆奔溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242990_comment'></div>再兴遂再进兵，于今月十四日到本县界孙洪涧，再逢张宣赞亲率贼马二千馀人，隔河相射，遂鼓率人马斗敌杀散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242990_comment'></div>至次日二更已来，收复长水县了当，夺到诸色粮斛二万馀石，给散百姓、官兵食用，即时招抚，并与安业，别无分毫搔扰，申乞照会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242990_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨<span class='inlineComment2'>（《金佗稡编》卷一六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242990_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1242990'>招抚并与安业别：原缺，据右引补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年8月</a>　遣王贵、郝政、董先，收复虢州卢氏县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年8月</a>　遣偏将收复商州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='eb2fef43cd3f4e3d9d0f477510f03580_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb2fef43cd3f4e3d9d0f477510f03580");'><span id='eb2fef43cd3f4e3d9d0f477510f03580_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年8月12日</a>　奉诏自襄阳起发赴行在。<br /></div>

新野（穰）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c5ae0132e7634b029c2b8de20b6d89bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c5ae0132e7634b029c2b8de20b6d89bc");'><span id='c5ae0132e7634b029c2b8de20b6d89bc_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，32岁</div><div id='7c3cce346b384ab9b6359030bebb2ec3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月17日</a>　复邓州，作捷奏。作品：《邓州捷奏》<div id='poem_1242987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓州捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242987")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242987'>镇南军承宣使、神武后军统制、江南西路舒蕲州兼荆南鄂岳黄复州汉阳军德安府制置使臣岳飞状奏：契勘叛贼李成与金贼刘合孛堇、陕西番、伪贼兵，并聚于邓州西北，劄三十馀寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242987_comment'></div>臣遣发王贵等由光化路，张宪等由横林路，前去掩杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242987_comment'></div>据统制王贵、张宪等申：「七月十五日，离邓州三十馀里，逢贼兵共数万接战，分遣王万、董先军兵，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242987", 1242987, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>出奇</span>突击，其贼大溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242987_comment'></div>降到番官杨德胜等二百馀人，夺马二百馀疋，衣甲不知其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242987_comment'></div>内高仲将一项残零人马，走入邓州，闭门坚守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242987_comment'></div>十七日，攻邓州，将士不顾矢石，蚁附而上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242987_comment'></div>破邓州，杀死番、伪贼马，鏖战大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242987_comment'></div>为暑月疲劳，见起发前去德安府歇泊，听候朝廷指挥外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242987_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

class='authorDate'>（1134年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242904")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242904'>清远军节度使、神武后军统制、充湖北路荆襄潭州制置使臣岳飞状奏：据襄阳府路安抚使司契勘，本路州县系居极边，全藉当职官协力措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242904_comment'></div>数内下项官并系收复之初，蒙制置司并本司逐急差权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242904_comment'></div>自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242904", 1242904, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>管当</span>事务以来，爱民无扰，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242904", 1242904, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>治职</span>有方，实堪倚仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242904_comment'></div>欲望详酌申奏，差补施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242904_comment'></div>今开具下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1242904'>一、借保义郎、襄阳府兵马监押王升，借迪功郎、襄阳府观察推官李霖，借迪功郎、襄阳府司理参军周冲翼，忠翊郎、襄阳府司法参军姚禾，成忠郎借忠翊郎、监。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>上疏条具宽恤荆襄诸措施。作品：《荆襄宽恤画一奏》<div id='poem_1242905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆襄宽恤画一奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242905")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242905'><span class='inlineComment2'>（以上原阙）</span>有科率及差借夫、马之类，许人户越诉，当职官吏乞赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1242905'>一、契勘人户归业之初，委是贫乏，全阙牛具、子种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242905_comment'></div>欲乞量借官钱，应副收买，候将来合纳税日，将所借官钱分四料，随税送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1242905'>一、契勘新复州军，其税赋依赦降指挥，权放三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242905_comment'></div>所有养赡官兵钱粮，无所从出，若不给降，深恐因循，却致扰民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242905_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷支降钱米，应副收籴，并借贷耕牛、子种、本钱，所贵归业之民得沾实惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1242905'>一、契勘新复州军城壁、楼橹并合修葺，防城器具并合置造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242905_comment'></div>所有合用钱粮，伏乞朝廷特赐支降，贵得应时办集，军民两安，不致疏虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1242905'>一、契勘人户未归业以前，应欠官私债负，不以是何名色，乞并行蠲放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242905_comment'></div>如州县辄敢理索，乞重赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1242905'>一、契勘新复州军全藉官员葺治，若不稍加恩数，深恐无以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1242905", 1242905, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>劝谕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242905_comment'></div>今相度欲乞几年为任，与转一官，选人比类施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242905_comment'></div>任满无遗阙，更与转一官，选人改合入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242905_comment'></div>应权官权过月日，理为实历月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1242905'>一、契勘新收复州军自合体认朝廷惠养宽恤之意，用心存抚，务令安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242905_comment'></div>欲乞令逐一开具元管并后来归业人户单甲、姓名，所住乡村，开垦过田土顷亩帐状，申本司审覆，诣实申奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242905_comment'></div>仍乞以召集多寡分数，立为殿最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1242905'>一、契勘所收复州军久经残害，上下凋弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242905_comment'></div>州县官如能用心召集流亡，劝课农桑，怀柔百姓，宽恤刑禁，从本司<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1242905", 1242905, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>保明</span>申奏，乞朝廷优异推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242905_comment'></div>若职事不虔，亦乞重赐黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242905_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1242905'>右画一条具在前，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1242905_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='36f55a7144e14bdb9160bccfcfaaa0cb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("36f55a7144e14bdb9160bccfcfaaa0cb");'><span id='36f55a7144e14bdb9160bccfcfaaa0cb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，33岁</div><div id='36f55a7144e14bdb9160bccfcfaaa0cb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月1日</a>　刘康年妄有陈请，上疏请夺其襄汉功。作品：《劾刘康年伪奏乞恩泽奏》<div id='poem_1242940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>劾刘康年伪奏乞恩泽奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242940")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242940'>清远军节度使、神武后军统制、充湖北路荆襄潭州制置使臣岳飞状奏：臣近读池州送到朝报，内一项系臣画一陈乞臣母封国夫人，第二项次男雷乞授文资，第三项乞江州庐山东林禅寺住持僧慧海佛心禅师事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242940_comment'></div>臣伏读，不胜惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242940_comment'></div>盖臣先于鄂州驻劄日，遣本军提举事务、武功大夫刘康年将收复襄汉等赏功文字，前去行在投进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242940_comment'></div>臣以鄂州去行在遥远，恐往复迟缓，又臣本军军器阙少，战马倒死者甚多，遂令刘康年赍空名印纸，因便将带陈乞军器、战马等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242940_comment'></div>不谓刘康年将前项印纸擅行书填，陈乞臣之私事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242940_comment'></div>窃念臣冗贱凡才，误蒙陛下擢任，兢兢旦夕，每虞不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242940_comment'></div>如臣近者蒙恩以收复襄汉六州，宠加旄节，臣凡五具恳辞，不敢祗受，虑或取诮公论，有玷清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242940_comment'></div>敢谓康年遽上此请，方当国家多事之际，陛下宵衣旰食，亲御六师，经理戎政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242940_comment'></div>臣虽至愚极陋，岂不知捐身效命，少图补报，况复敢以私门猥琐，希求恩宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242940_comment'></div>臣若不披露肝胆，力为辨雪，天下其谓臣何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242940_comment'></div>伏望陛下察臣悃愊，实未尝敢萌此意，乞将上件恩数早赐追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242940_comment'></div>仍将刘康年妄行书填印纸情罪，明正朝典，所有臣不合令刘康年将带空名印纸事理，见在本军待罪，伏乞同赐黜责施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242940_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1242940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月</a>　再次乞求追寝刘康年妄请之恩泽。作品：《再乞寝罢刘康年伪乞恩泽札子》<div id='poem_1242941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞寝罢刘康年伪乞恩泽劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242941")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242941'>清远军节度使、神武后军统制、充湖北路荆襄潭州制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：契勘臣近于正月初一日尝具奏，闻为本军提举一行事务官、武功大夫刘康年妄行书填印纸，乞母封国夫人，次男雷换文资，僧慧海禅师事，乞赐追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242941_comment'></div>仍将刘康年妄行书填印纸情罪，明正朝典，所有臣不合令刘康年将带印纸事理，臣见在本军待罪，乞同赐黜责施行去后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242941_comment'></div>今月十七日准尚书省劄子：「正月八日，三省同奉圣旨，岳飞放罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242941_comment'></div>刘康年罢神武后军提举一行事务，依冲替人例施行，系事理重，仍追夺收复襄汉等赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242941_comment'></div>飞母封号系是特恩，可依已降指挥，馀令改正」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242941_comment'></div>臣以猥琐之资，曲荷天地广大之恩，终不加罪，保全微臣，臣虽殒身，无以仰报圣德万分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242941_comment'></div>重念臣奋迹单微，今来滥厕承流，于法母已是当封淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242941_comment'></div>遭际陛下，实为荣幸，岂敢踰分，过有邀求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242941_comment'></div>前三事上感睿照，特赐辨明，皆已施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242941_comment'></div>独有臣母国夫人号，未蒙改正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242941_comment'></div>窃惟国家封爵，自有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1242941", 1242941, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>彝制</span>，岂可躐等超迁，有紊旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242941_comment'></div>若因刘康年妄有陈请，陛下必欲以此封臣之母，不惟臣终不遑安，亦于公论不以为允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242941_comment'></div>伏望圣慈洞察，怜臣勤恳之诚，俯从所欲，将臣母特封国号事，速赐追还，以正名分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242941_comment'></div>取进止/〔贴黄〕如以为特恩不可复夺，乞将飞旄钺恩数追寝，回授施行，庶几不致滥受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242941_comment'></div>伏乞睿照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1242941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月1日</a>　赏淮西之功，晋封母姚氏为福国夫人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年春</a>　游翠微亭，纵情大自然，有诗。作品：《池州翠微亭》<div id='poem_166909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>池州翠微亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_166909")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_166909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166909'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166909'>经年尘土满征衣，特特寻芳上翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_166909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_166909'>好山好水看不足，马蹄催趁月明归<span class='inlineComment2'>（明徐阶辑《岳武穆集》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_166909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_166909'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_166909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年春</a>　游翠光亭，作诗抒思归之意。作品：《翠光亭》<div id='poem_166921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_166921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/166921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题池州翠光寺<span class='inlineComment2'>（《式古堂书画汇考》卷一三作亭）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_166921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_166921'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_166921'>爱此倚栏杆，谁同寓目閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166921'>予虽江上老，心羡白云还<span class='inlineComment2'>（《式古堂书画汇考》作关）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_166921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年8月</a>　由襄阳往临安时，路经池州，不满和议，再上章求退。作品：《奏乞致仕第二札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（据《乞致仕第三札子》文意，《乞致仕第一札子》（已佚）当作于过江州时，《乞致仕第二札子》作于池州，《乞致仕第三札子》作于广德军。）</span><br /></div>

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年12月</a>　败金人于庐州，作申省状。作品：《庐州捷报申省状》<div id='poem_1243067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐州捷报申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243067")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243067'>清远军节度使、湖北路荆襄潭州制置使岳飞状申：据统制官徐庆、牛皋申：「部押人马，前来庐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243067_comment'></div>到本州安泊未定间，有番、伪贼兵逼近州城，遂躬亲率所统人马出城，迎捍斗敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243067_comment'></div>自申时转战至酉时，其贼败走，大获胜捷，杀戮贼兵三十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243067_comment'></div>除杀死并斩首级外，活擒到番、伪贼兵八十馀人，夺到马八十馀匹，枪刀不知其数目，贼马<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1243067", 1243067, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>走透</span>前去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243067_comment'></div>飞契勘元差徐庆、牛皋等将带官兵二千馀人，前去庐、寿、濠州、天长军以来，掩击贼马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243067_comment'></div>今到庐州城下，逢贼战斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243067_comment'></div>除在城内及在城南下寨官兵更不开具外，今具接战实立功官兵五百四十六人，分为等第，谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏乞照会施行，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243067_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='db47f673ae03409386bfa4c66660d700_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("db47f673ae03409386bfa4c66660d700");'><span id='db47f673ae03409386bfa4c66660d700_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月</a>　师至庐州。<br /></div>
-----end

class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242957_comment'></div>蝼蚁之诚，未回天听，不免再沥忱恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242957_comment'></div>伏念臣顷自天下兵兴时，实有志于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242957", 1242957, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>奋张</span>皇威，削平僭乱，以为北虏不灭，臣死不瞑，初不敢萌觊觎高爵厚禄之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242957_comment'></div>既而误蒙陛下使令，付以兵柄责任以来，荏苒积年，腥膻叛逆之族，尚据中土，而臣之官职岁迁月转，岂不有负初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242957_comment'></div>兼臣见今官职不为不崇，岂容一向叨窃，不自愧耻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242957_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐哀矜，察臣愚衷，收还大命，庶令臣得勉力事功，以酬素抱，以报厚恩，不犯盈满颠隮之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242957_comment'></div>所有告命，臣未敢祗受，见寄纳平江府军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242957_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年2月</a>　第三次上章辞太尉。作品：《辞太尉第三札子》<div id='poem_1242960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞太尉第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242960")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242960'>起复检校少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚副使兼营田使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣近两具奏，乞追寝太尉恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242960_comment'></div>今月二十九日准尚书省劄子，二月二十八日奉圣旨，依已降诏旨，不允，不得再有陈请，令日下祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242960_comment'></div>臣一介么微，言语鄙浅，不能上格天听，用敢不避再三，荐控诚悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242960_comment'></div>臣顷以目疾，废事日久，近者商、虢、颍、蔡之战，皆由仰遵圣训，遂致将士竭力，在臣实无寸功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242960_comment'></div>且太尉掌武之官，授非其人，则不足以为今日右武之劝，臣若谬居不辞，是因臣一己而怠天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242960_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特回渊鉴，收还误恩，令臣只以见官待罪军旅，庶几天下始知大官之为可重，不累陛下立政惟人之明，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242960_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242960_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_title_1242903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242903'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242903'><span class='inlineComment2'>（以上原阙）</span>禹节制使唤，事毕遣还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242903_comment'></div>荆南镇抚司并湖南帅司各发兵、船，约期进讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242903_comment'></div>下流合用军兵，及会合诸头项兵马、舟船，并委飞措置施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242903_comment'></div>所有岳飞本军合用钱粮，如所部州军应副不足，依旧朝廷给降，及江西路支拨应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242903_comment'></div>劄送臣疾速施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242903_comment'></div>臣伏蒙新除恩命，已具奏辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242903_comment'></div>所有措置讨捕黄诚、杨太等贼徒事，切缘臣所管军马，并系西北之人，不习水战，今蒙圣旨驱使，不敢辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242903_comment'></div>谨已遵奉指挥外，臣契勘湖贼黄诚、杨太等占据重湖，猖獗累年，战舰、舟船数目浩瀚，又贼众多凭恃水险，出没作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242903_comment'></div>今来若以湖南帅司马准、步谅两项军马听知鼎州程昌禹节制，以荆南镇抚司并湖南帅司各发兵、船，约期进讨，切虑如此事不专一，临时难以措画，有误指踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242903_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈特降睿旨，令湖南帅司除留三千人在潭州弹压外，并荆南镇抚司都共有二千人，乞令臣量留一千人在镇抚司外，将其馀军马、舟船，尽数并拨付臣相度分布使唤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242903_comment'></div>兼马准、步谅亦乞令付臣使唤，如鼎州缓急合要军马使用，乞令臣相度分遣，庶几军马归一，斟量调发，免致误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242903_comment'></div>兼契勘王𤫉已降指挥，江州驻劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242903_comment'></div>今来讨捕湖贼，正赖舟船使用，欲乞将王𤫉随军舟船，除海船及有馀船外，只乞战船并海湖船，权暂尽数借拨付本军，候事毕日归还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242903_comment'></div>臣访闻湖南州郡系出产材木去处，欲乞行下本路，一就并钉线工匠，应副添修本军舟船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242903_comment'></div>其合用钱粮，窃详湖北路委是阙乏，无以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1242903", 1242903, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>桩办</span>，伏乞特降指挥，专一令江西应副外，券钱乞从朝廷宽剩支降，贵不有误事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242903_comment'></div>所陈利害，并系急切，伏望圣慈详酌，依臣所乞，前去措画，誓尽犬马之劳，以图报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1242903_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1242903_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1242903'>〔贴黄〕臣契勘湖贼先与伪贼结连，近探得陕府、长安见今点集人马，东京亦已聚兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1242903_comment'></div>今来襄汉诸州并系边面，防秋是时，切虑不测，前来侵犯作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1242903_comment'></div>伏乞添兵屯守，及更抽摘军马，付臣遣发巡边照管，庶免误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1242903_comment'></div>乞速赐措置施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1242903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月17日</a>　诏飞治军有法，令学士院降诏奖谕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月</a>　上章乞请田明充衡州兵马钤辖，以安恤受降起义首领。作品：《乞田明添差申都督府状》<div id='poem_1243042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243042' class='poemTitle class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243042")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243042'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路制置使岳飞状申：恭奉圣旨，措置招捕荆湖南、北路盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243042_comment'></div>其王太尉先与水战见阵，少却之后，有首领田明率众前来荆湖南、北路安抚司<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1243042", 1243042, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>出首</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243042_comment'></div>虽蒙朝廷将田明补武义大夫、荣州刺史、兼閤门宣赞舍人，然至今未沾寸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243042_comment'></div>深虑无以劝诱自新之人，伏望特赐指挥，添差田明充衡州兵马钤辖一次，庶几改过之人得以安恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243042_comment'></div>谨具申都督府，伏候指挥。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月</a>　黄佐袭周伦寨，败之。申都督行府增补黄佐官武经大夫，依前閤门宣赞舍人。作品：《增补黄佐官申都督府状》<div id='poem_1243043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>增补黄佐官申都督府状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年4月）</span><span id='poem_sentence_1_1243043_comment'></div>今据黄佐申：「今年四月十四日到周伦寨与贼斗敌，除当下杀死及掩入湖贼徒甚众，并投到统制陈贵等九人，夺到衣甲不算，掩取寨栅粮船了当」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243043_comment'></div>契勘黄佐首先掩杀周伦贼非徒获捷，委是忠义勇敢，理宜旌赏，已将朝廷降到空名告，依便宜指挥书填武经大夫，依前閤门宣赞舍人，给付黄佐祗领外，谨请申都督府，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1243043_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242989'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路制置使臣岳飞状奏：近差统制官任士安部押军马，前去□□□□□措置把截黄诚等贼马去后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242989_comment'></div>据任士安申：「五月五□□□□□□伪太子、渠魁黄诚等节次前来侵犯永安寨，其贼□□□□□□匹、步军二万馀人，摆拽十馀里，与官兵相拒斗敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242989_comment'></div>□□□□□□率亲兵，并武功郎、统领陈照人马，分路会合，至永□□□□□□阵，前来迎敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242989_comment'></div>任士安引兵当头冲击，贼徒败走，夺□□□□□，黏踪追袭，过苟陂山，杀死甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242989_comment'></div>夺到衣甲、器械，捉到贼人马，见别具状供申外，委是大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242989_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_title_1243057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243057'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243057'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖北襄阳府路制置使岳飞状申：准都督行府劄子：「勘会制置使司近差官兵平荡湖贼了当，内奇功、第一等人并已推恩讫，其武翼郎、閤门宣赞舍人岳云亦系奇功，缘云系岳飞之子，不曾保明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243057_comment'></div>除已具奏，乞优与推恩外，劄付飞照会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243057_comment'></div>契勘今来平荡湖贼，并系将士戮力用命之功，男云虽曾随军前去，即不曾立到显效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243057_comment'></div>所有前项行府照劄，飞即不敢令男云祗受，今随状缴纳，乞不施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243057_comment'></div>谨具申都督行府，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243057_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月18日</a>　诏兼蕲黄州制置使，以目疾乞解军事，乞除一在外宫观。作品：《乞宫祠 札子》<br /><a showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242944")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242944'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣于六月十八日尝具奏劄，冒犯天聪，惟切震惧，朝夕恭俟宸命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242944_comment'></div>今月十九日准尚书省劄子：「奉圣旨，岳飞已平<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242944", 1242944, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>湖湘</span>，见措置上流事务，责任繁重，所请不允，仍不得再有陈请者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242944_comment'></div>伏念臣起身田野，势援孤单，荷陛下天地父母之恩，曲垂覆育，虽臣捐躯效死，岂足以图报万分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242944_comment'></div>臣前所请，固非忍为，亦非所愿，寔以臣垂白之亲，别无兼侍，年来多病，颇觉羸瘠，又臣先所染瘴，缘冒暑毒，今亦未瘥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242944_comment'></div>虽平居无事，犹恐不能任责，况今日上流形势，所系至重，若非智谋宏远、勇略过人者，安能分陛下宵旰之忧，仰副委寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242944_comment'></div>如臣不才，冒滥宠荣，加以抱疾而不知止，终恐有误使令，上贻陛下忧顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242944_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣愚恳，不敢饰辞，早赐俞允，除臣一在外宫观差遣，苟免颠隮，实出生成之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242944_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1242944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　作状陈平湖南寇事宜。作品：《平湖寇申省状》<div id='poem_1243068' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　第三次上章乞宫祠。作品：《乞宫祠第三札子》<div id='poem_1242945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠第三劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242945")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242945'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242945'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：先具诚恳，冒渎天聪，乞一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242945_comment'></div>准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，不允，仍不得再有陈请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242945_comment'></div>伏念臣起自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242945", 1242945, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>白丁</span>，误蒙器使，仰荷圣慈委曲异眷，虽父母之爱其子，何以复加，顾臣之事陛下，岂不愿殚竭疲驽，以毕此生，仰图报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242945_comment'></div>况今防秋是时，讵敢托以他事，觊安闲退？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242945_comment'></div>实缘臣老母垂白多病，又臣渐染瘴疾，四肢堕废，两目昏赤，而臣职掌兵戎，系国利害，莫大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242945_comment'></div>臣若贪冒荣宠，昧于进退，不哀鸣控告于君父，在臣一身，固不足惜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242945_comment'></div>重念朝廷付以上流，责任不轻，恐致颠隮，有误委寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242945_comment'></div>伏望睿照矜其愚悃，别无规避，特降指挥，检会臣前所陈请，早赐俞允，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242945_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1242945_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月19日</a>　诏不许乞在外宫观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年8月3日</a>　诏飞军以三十将为额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年9月12日</a>　加检校少保，食邑五百户，实封二百户，进封鄂国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年10月</a>　上章再辞检校少保。作品：《辞检校少保第二札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《辞检校少保第一札子》已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞检校少保第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span "poem_title_1242946")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242946'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路蕲黄州制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比具辞免检校少保恩命事，今月十五日，伏蒙圣恩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242946", 1242946, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>曲降</span>诏谕，未赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242946_comment'></div>臣义有未尽，跼蹐靡皇，辄敢再羾丹诚，仰干渊听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242946_comment'></div>伏念臣本无才术，误膺眷渥，未能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242946", 1242946, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>攘却</span>夷狄，扫除<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242946", 1242946, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>僭窃</span>，以副陛下削平祸乱之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1242946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1242946'><span class='label'>按：</span>以下原阙　《金佗稡编》卷一三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1242946_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年11月</a>　第四次上章辞检校少保。作品：《辞检校少保第四札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《辞检校少保第三札子》已佚。）</span><div id='poem_1242948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞检校少保第四劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242948")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242948'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路蕲黄州制置使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比具辞免除臣检校少保恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242948_comment'></div>今月初一日再准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，依已降诏旨，不允，不得再有陈请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242948_comment'></div>伏念臣已三贡辞章，出于诚悃，冒犯天威，罪不容赦，圣恩广大，一赐温诏，两降劄命，扪心揣分，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242948_comment'></div>伏念臣草芥固陋，备数<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242948", 1242948, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>戎昭</span>，曾无尺寸之功，仰报天地之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242948_comment'></div>窃以亚保之位，实预三孤之贵，所以赏有功而进豪杰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242948_comment'></div>如臣何人，辄膺斯宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242948_comment'></div>是以心不自安，终难冒受，不避谴诛，再伸前恳，非敢徒为辞逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242948_comment'></div>伏望圣慈矜察愚衷，早还成命，庶令臣少安分守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242948_comment'></div>臣不胜虔祈俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242948_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1242948_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
常德（武陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='258716a239a24e8cbdda104ea0a6d04a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("258716a239a24e8cbdda104ea0a6d04a");'><span id='258716a239a24e8cbdda104ea0a6d04a_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年5月25日</a>　至鼎州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月2日</a>　黄佐招杨钦来降。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　上章奏招杨钦事。作品：《招杨钦奏》<div id='poem_1242906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招杨钦奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242906'>镇宁崇信军节度使、神武后军都统制、荆湖南北襄阳府路制置使臣岳飞状奏：恭奉圣旨，措置荆湖南、北路盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242906_comment'></div>臣遂先分遣军马，扼贼要路，断其粮道，严行禁止博易，使贼乏食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242906_comment'></div>寻遣军分头赍执旗、榜，谕以祸福，说谕招安，溃其腹心，并欲诱致桀黠，以为乡导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242906_comment'></div>今据武义大夫、閤门宣赞舍人黄佐等招安水寨首领杨钦，将带到本寨徒众老小约一万馀人、大小舟船八百馀只、牛五百馀头、马四十馀疋，并到军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242906_comment'></div>臣已优加存抚，及即时支破钱粮养赡，并先次将空名武义大夫告书填，给付杨钦了当，所有以次头领亦见行取会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242906_comment'></div>契勘杨钦系贼之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1242906", 1242906, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>密党</span>，今已服从，正宜乘机掩覆巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242906_comment'></div>臣一面措置进兵外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　作状陈招杨钦事。作品：《招安杨钦等申都督行府状》<div id='poem_1243044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招安杨钦等申都督行府状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1243044_comment'></div>除已优加存恤外，谨具申都督行府，伏乞照会，谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1243044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月11日</a>　破杨幺于洞庭湖。<br /></div>

-----title
汝南（汝阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='273a0c864bdc4aaea2c2f4f161d86152_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("273a0c864bdc4aaea2c2f4f161d86152");'><span id='273a0c864bdc4aaea2c2f4f161d86152_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='273a0c864bdc4aaea2c2f4f161d86152' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　领兵援刘锜，与金人战于蔡州，复蔡州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4ac94115c446451bb07477b1825f8b00_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ac94115c446451bb07477b1825f8b00");'><span id='4ac94115c446451bb07477b1825f8b00_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='4ac94115c446451bb07477b1825f8b00' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>以赵秉渊知淮宁府事，作申省状。作品：《差赵秉渊知淮宁府申省状》<div id='poem_1243055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>差赵秉渊知淮宁府申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243055")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243055'>少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使岳飞状申：契勘飞近为权知淮宁府刘永寿、史贵擅弃淮宁府城，已将逐官依军法行遣，及申奏朝廷，乞将逐官更赐行遣外，飞遂差统制官赵秉渊将带军马，前去措置占守去后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243055_comment'></div>今据赵秉渊申，已于七月二十三日军马入淮宁府城，安贴官吏、居民讫，申乞照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243055_comment'></div>所有淮宁府伏望特降指挥，下淮北宣抚司差官施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243055_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省并枢密院，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1243055_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复颍昌府奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年闰6月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242991")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242991'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：据前军统制、同提举一行事务张宪申：「统率军马，前去措置贼马，除于闰六月十九日离颍昌府四十里，与番贼见阵获捷外，宪复统率军马，追袭贼帅韩常，其贼大败，于当月二十日收复颍昌府了当」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242991_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1242991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年闰6月25日</a>　遣张宪复陈州，颍昌再败金兵，上章奏捷。作品：《陈州颍昌捷奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（淮宁府即陈州。）</span><div id='poem_1242992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州颍昌捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年闰6月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242992")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242992'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今据诸军申到收复下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242992'>一、据前军统制张宪申：「将带诸统制、将官前去措置陈州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242992_comment'></div>闰六月二十四日午时，离陈州十五里，逢贼马军三千馀骑见阵掩杀，其众望城奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242992_comment'></div>遂分诸头项并进，离城数里，有番贼翟将军等，并添到东京一带差来贼马，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242992", 1242992, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>摆布</span>大阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242992_comment'></div>宪遂鼓率将士，分头入阵掩击，其贼败走，已收复陈州了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242992_comment'></div>除杀死外，生擒到番贼王太保等，并夺到鞍马等，委获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242992_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1242992'>一、据踏白军统制董先、游奕军统制姚政等申：「统率军马，在颍昌府驻劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242992_comment'></div>闰六月二十五日辰时，有番贼取长葛县路前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242992_comment'></div>先即时同姚政等统率军马，出城迎敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242992_comment'></div>到城北七里店，逢镇国大王并韩将军、邪也孛堇贼马六千馀骑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1242992", 1242992, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>摆布</span>成阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242992_comment'></div>先与姚政等分头项径入贼阵，战斗及一时辰，其贼败走，追杀三十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242992_comment'></div>除杀死外，擒到人并夺到鞍马等，委获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242992_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1242992'>右谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1242992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年闰6月25日</a>　遣郝晸等复郑州，上章奏捷。作品：《郑州捷奏》<div id='poem_1242993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242993' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_1242993'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：据中军统制王贵申：「先次遣将杨成等统率军马，前去措置郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242993_comment'></div>今据杨成等申：于闰六月二十五日到郑州南，逢番贼头领漫独化等部领贼马五千馀人见阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242993_comment'></div>成等遂鼓率将士，与贼见阵，掩杀贼马败走，收郑州，抚定了当，委获胜捷」。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年闰6月27日</a>　秦桧召刘锜还，上章乞请刘锜依旧屯顺昌。作品：《乞刘锜依旧屯顺昌奏》<div id='poem_1242921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242921' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_1242921_comment'></div>右三省、枢密院同奉圣旨，令岳飞依已降指挥，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242921", 1242921, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>辟差</span>顺昌府守臣，日下具名闻奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242921_comment'></div>劄送臣疾速施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242921_comment'></div>臣除已恭依前项圣旨指挥施行外，臣契勘近准枢密院劄子节文：「奉圣旨，顺昌府旧属京西，合拨属本路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242921_comment'></div>并要岳飞分拨兵将，严为守备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242921_comment'></div>刘锜候岳飞差到兵马，将所部起发，前去镇江府，听候指挥使唤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242921_comment'></div>本司契勘所管军马，已分布调发前去陕、虢、西京、陈、蔡、颍昌、汝、郑州一带，并已有差往河东、河北措置事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242921_comment'></div>已两次申奏，乞将刘锜一军且令于顺昌府屯驻，庶几缓急可以照应去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242921_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，依臣已申奏事理施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242921_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1242921_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='437cab276fe4434a968275bf73f41462_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月2日</a>　上章请追寝少保册命。作品：《辞册命札子》<div id='poem_1242974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞册命劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242974")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242974'>少保、武胜定国军节度使、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比准制命，授臣少保，累具辞免，伏蒙圣慈降诏不允，不得再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242974_comment'></div>臣不避斧钺之诛，再露丹诚，仰干天听，乞赐追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242974_comment'></div>又于今月初一日奉圣旨指挥閤门，岳飞除少保，累具辞免，已降指挥不允，日下祗受，不得再有陈请，可令便立新班，特放告正谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242974_comment'></div>臣已于今月初二日望阙谢恩祗受讫，所有册命恩数，伏望睿旨许免，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242974_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1242974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月2日</a>　遣张应、韩清等将收复西京，上章奏捷。作品：《复西京奏》<div id='poem_sentence_0_1242995_comment'></div>今据郝晸等申：进发至离西京六十里下寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242995_comment'></div>于七月初一日，有金贼马军数千骑前来，即时差将官张应、韩清将带马军，于贼来路把截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242995_comment'></div>其贼前来迎敌官军，张应等即时掩杀，贼马败走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242995_comment'></div>晸进发军马，当日酉时直凑西京城下。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月7日</a>　遣杨遇等将复南城，上章奏捷。作品：《复南城军捷奏》<div id='poem_1242997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_1242997_comment'></div>所有夺到鞍马、舟船、器甲、弓、箭、旗、枪等别具状供申外，逼逐贼兵出城，上船渡河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242997_comment'></div>至初七日收复南城军了当，已抚存官吏、居民，各安职业。<div class='inline' -----title
中牟（长社）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6c7b3b2ce6a24dc8a30c7f05c897ad20_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c7b3b2ce6a24dc8a30c7f05c897ad20");'><span id='6c7b3b2ce6a24dc8a30c7f05c897ad20_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='6c7b3b2ce6a24dc8a30c7f05c897ad20' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年闰6月29日</a>　于中牟县破金漫独化军寨，上章奏捷。作品：《漫独化捷奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作《奏中牟县捷状》）</span><div id='poem_1242994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漫独化捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年闰6月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242994")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242994'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：据本司中军统制王贵申：「据准备将刘政等申：将带人兵，于闰六月二十九日夜，劫破中牟县金贼万户漫独化贼寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242994_comment'></div>杀死贼兵不知数目，夺到马三百五十馀匹，驴、骡一百馀头，衣物、器甲等不计数目，即未知万户漫独化存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242994_comment'></div>委获胜捷，申乞照会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242994_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242994_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
漯河（郾城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='773cbd7178c84f5fb272460ca4a59b3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("773cbd7178c84f5fb272460ca4a59b3d");'><span id='773cbd7178c84f5fb272460ca4a59b3d_link' id='poem_title_1242996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242996'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今月初八日，探得有番贼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242996", 1242996, "Clauses/2/Comments/3")'>酋首</span>四太子、龙虎、盖天大王、韩将军亲领马军一万五千馀骑，例各鲜明衣甲，取径路，离郾城县北二十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242996_comment'></div>寻遣发背嵬、游奕马军，自申时后，与贼战斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242996_comment'></div>将士各持麻扎刀、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242996", 1242996, "Clauses/9/Comments/2")'>提刀</span>、大斧，与贼手拽厮劈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242996_comment'></div>鏖战数十合，杀死贼兵满野，不计其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242996_comment'></div>至天色昏黑，方始贼兵退，那夺到马二百馀匹，委获大捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242996_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1242996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月10日</a>　败宗弼于郾城北五里店，上章奏捷。作品：《郾城县北并垣曲等捷奏》<div id='poem_1242998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郾城县北并垣曲县等捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242998")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242998'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使、兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今月初十日申时，据<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242998", 1242998, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>巡绰马</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242998", 1242998, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>报覆</span>，有番贼马军一千馀骑，径来侵犯郾城县北五里店，在后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1242998", 1242998, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>尘头</span>不绝，不知数目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242998_comment'></div>臣躬亲提领军马，出城迎敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242998_comment'></div>遣差背嵬将官王刚等，将带背嵬使臣五十馀人骑，前去探贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242998_comment'></div>据王刚等称，于五里店见贼摆一字阵，内见一名甲上着紫袍，认是头领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242998_comment'></div>遂一齐入贼军，并手斫下上件头领，其馀贼众一发退走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242998_comment'></div>今于斫下尸首上并马鬃上，取到红漆牌子二个，上题写「阿李朵孛堇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242998_comment'></div>追赶贼马二十馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242998_comment'></div>当日又据本司统领忠义军马梁兴、董荣申：「依准指挥，统押军马前来，过大河剿杀金贼，占夺州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242998_comment'></div>兴等于今月初一日晚，到黄河南岸，措置济河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242998_comment'></div>其黄河北岸有金贼三十馀人骑，于岸口摆列阵势，守备人马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242998_comment'></div>兴等于初二日早领兵，与统领董荣等人马渡河，到北岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242998_comment'></div>贼马就岸交战，其贼败走，追赶入绛州垣曲县，闭门拒敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242998_comment'></div>兴等遂行张榜说谕，不肯归降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242998_comment'></div>至午时，兴等领兵，与统领董荣等人马措置绞缚云梯，一齐上城<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1242998", 1242998, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>接战</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1242998_comment'></div>杀死番贼不知数目，活捉到千户刘来孙等一十四人，并夺到战马一百馀匹、器仗等，见行抚存人户安业，依旧种作外，申乞照会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1242998_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1242998_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b781f22e2cfe49ecad1890eacf60ac01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b781f22e2cfe49ecad1890eacf60ac01");'><span id='b781f22e2cfe49ecad1890eacf60ac01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='b781f22e2cfe49ecad1890eacf60ac01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月14日</a>　王贵等于颖昌杀宗弼婿统军上将军夏金吾，上章奏捷。作品：《王贵颍昌捷奏》<div id='poem_1243001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王贵颍昌捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243001")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243001'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今月十五日，据本司中军统制、提举一行事务王贵申：「依准指挥，统率诸军人马，于颍昌府屯驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243001_comment'></div>今月十四日辰时以来，有番贼四太子、镇国大王、并昭武大将军韩常及番贼万户四人，亲领番兵马军三万馀骑，直抵颍昌府西门外摆列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243001_comment'></div>贵遂令踏白军统制董先、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1243001", 1243001, "Clauses/10/Comments/1")'>选锋</span>军副统制胡清守城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243001_comment'></div>贵亲统中军、游奕军人马，并机宜岳云将带到背嵬军出城迎战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243001_comment'></div>自辰时至午时，血战数十合，当阵杀死万户一人、千户五人，贼兵横尸满野，约五百馀人，重伤番贼不知数目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243001_comment'></div>其夺到战马、金鼓、旗、枪、器甲等不计其数，见行根刷，续具数目供申次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243001_comment'></div>委是大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243001_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1243001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　上章奏河北诸捷。作品：《河北诸捷奏》<div id='poem_1243000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河北颍昌诸捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243000")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243000'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今月十五日，据本司统领忠义军马梁兴、赵云、李进并董荣、牛显、张峪申：「依准指挥，将带人马过河，占夺州县，掩杀金贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243000_comment'></div>兴等除已于七月初二日收复绛州垣曲县了当，已行供申外，兴等统押军马，至七月初四日到孟州王屋县界，地名西阳、邵源，驻劄两寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243000_comment'></div>汉儿军张太保等部押手下汉军人马六十馀人，前来投降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243000_comment'></div>至初五日辰时，到王屋县西，地名东阳，有驻劄北军一寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243000_comment'></div>为兴等统兵前去，其贼弃寨逃走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243000_comment'></div>当日午时，统率军马到王屋县，贼马为兴等人马逼近，并已弃城逃走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243000_comment'></div>兴等人马不曾入城，乘势追赶贼马二十馀里，夺到战马八匹，杀死贼兵三十馀人，并夺到衣、甲、刀、枪、旗帜无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243000_comment'></div>兴等差人招诱王屋县百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1243000", 1243000, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>首领</span>王璋等五十馀人，当面出给旗、榜，招集本县逃走军民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1243000", 1243000, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>着业</span>去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243000_comment'></div>至初六日，统兵到孟州济源县西，地名曲阳二十里以来，逢金贼高太尉贼马五千馀人骑前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243000_comment'></div>兴等躬亲统押人马，分头前去迎敌，与贼血战，自辰时及午时，其贼大败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243000_comment'></div>杀死金贼，一十馀里横尸遍野，并夺到器械、枪、刀、旗、鼓等无数，及活捉到金贼八十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243000_comment'></div>兴等收兵歇泊下寨间，至未时以来，有高太尉再将到怀、孟、卫等州界发来贼马一万馀人骑，分布前来兴等对面，摆阵相拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243000_comment'></div>兴等即时分布军马，并力与贼迎敌，不顾死生血战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243000_comment'></div>自未至酉时，剿杀金贼步军八分已上，夺到战马、驴、骡二百馀头匹，活捉到金贼一百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243000_comment'></div>追袭至县西门，其高太尉将带残零贼马退走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243000_comment'></div>兴等为官军尽日见阵，伤中数多，遂统押军马，前去本县北十馀里，地名燕川，歇泊下寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243000_comment'></div>委是大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243000_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1243000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　上章乞降付李兴、吴琦转官告。作品：《李兴吴琦转官告乞付军前给降奏》<div id='poem_1242918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李兴吴琦转官告乞付军前给降奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242918")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242918'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：契勘本司近据统领官梁兴申：「差人探报得河南府见被金贼占据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242918_comment'></div>本府有番人七千馀人、马五千馀匹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242918", 1242918, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>食粮</span>军三千馀人，知府系叛贼、伪奉国上将军、安武军节度使李成，并差番人同知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242918_comment'></div>其本府管下福昌、永宁、伊阳三县，番贼不曾前去，止有河南府钤辖李兴人兵往来，私掠财物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242918_comment'></div>及据伊阳县申，亦为上件李兴事理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242918_comment'></div>臣已差秉义郎加借武翼郎、閤门宣赞舍人、本司中军统领军马苏坚权河南府事，令择一县，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1242918", 1242918, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>寄治</span>府事，招收军马，措置事宜，及拘收李兴一行前来军前使唤外，伏望圣慈特降睿旨，付臣照会施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242918_comment'></div>所有李兴、吴琦转官告，乞给降付臣，候再立微效日给付施行，庶得有以激劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242918_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　上章乞号令归一，以备缓争。作品：《乞号令归一奏》<div id='poem_1242922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞号令归一奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242922")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242922'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：契勘武功大夫、果州团练使、知陕州军州事吴琦，本司于今年六月十三日差兼京西湖北宣抚使、河南北诸路招讨使司选锋军副统制，后来于闰六月二十六日改差兼撞军统制军马，令团集忠义人兵，与本司差去统制官措置掩杀金贼，收复州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242922_comment'></div>今据吴琦申：「准川、陕宣抚使司劄子，恭依圣旨，便宜黜陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242922_comment'></div>勘会陕州最系极边，其知州、武功大夫、果州团练使吴琦见纠集忠义军兵，据险保聚，捍敌金贼，理宜增重事权，今差兼管内安抚、统制忠义军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242922_comment'></div>除已奏闻外，仰准此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242922_comment'></div>除已祗受外，申乞照会」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242922_comment'></div>臣契勘川、陕宣抚使司差吴琦前项职事，委是与本司交互，事不归一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242922_comment'></div>兼虢州亦元属陕西，欲望圣慈特降睿旨，将虢州依旧拨隶川、陕宣抚司，其知虢州武赳并元带去军马，却乞发还本司，应副使唤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1242922_comment'></div>及寄理武功大夫、博州刺史、河南府兵马钤辖李兴，本司先次依已得圣旨便宜指挥，差兼本司左军统制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1242922_comment'></div>今据李兴申，准朝廷指挥，差知河南府、兼本路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1242922_comment'></div>今来措置事宜之间，照应不一，切恐有误指踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1242922_comment'></div>并蔡州、汝州近准朝廷拨隶京西南路，欲乞将逐州依旧拨隶河南府路，别差帅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1242922_comment'></div>并蕲、黄、光州元属淮西，亦乞并拨隶本路，庶几归一，缓急不致误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1242922_comment'></div>只乞令臣依旧为朝廷守湖北、京西两路，以备缓急使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1242922_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1242922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　连续大捷，乞诸路并进，实现中兴。作品：《乞乘机进兵札子》<div id='poem_1242919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞乘机进兵劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242919")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242919'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞劄子奏：臣比得卫州忠义统制赵俊差人赍到申状，自闰六月二十七日起离本州，于今月初四日到臣军前报，比遣兵过河，会合忠义统制乔握坚等，已收复赵州了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242919_comment'></div>又遣本司统制梁兴、董荣两军过河，河北州县往往自乱，民心皆愿归朝廷，乞遣发大兵，前来措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242919_comment'></div>臣契勘金贼近累败衄，其虏酋四太子等皆令老小渡河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242919_comment'></div>惟是贼众尚徘徊于京城南壁一带，近却发八千人过河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242919_comment'></div>此正是陛下中兴之机，乃金贼必亡之日，若不乘势殄灭，恐贻后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242919_comment'></div>伏望速降指挥，令诸路之兵火急并进，庶几早见成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242919_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月18日</a>　张宪之将徐庆、李山等复捷于临颖，上章奏捷。作品：《临颍捷奏》<div id='poem_1243002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临颍捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1243002")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243002'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：据本司前军统制、同提举一行事务张宪申：「今月十八日，到临颍县东北，逢金贼马军约五千骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243002_comment'></div>分遣统制徐庆、李山、寇成、傅选等马军一布向前，入阵与贼战斗，其贼败走，追赶十五馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243002_comment'></div>杀死贼兵横尸满野，夺到器甲等无数，轻骑牵到马一百馀匹，委是大获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243002_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1243002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月18日</a>　破兀术于朱仙镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月18日</a>　遣使修治陵寝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月18日</a>　有诏班师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月18日</a>　秦桧力主和议，下诏班师，上章奏乞止班师。作品：《乞止班师诏奏略》<div id='poem_1242923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞止班师诏奏略<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242923")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242923'>契勘金虏重兵尽聚东京，屡经败衄，锐气沮丧，内外震骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242923_comment'></div>闻之谍者，虏欲弃其辎重，疾走渡河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242923_comment'></div>况今豪杰向风，士卒用命，天时人事，强弱已见，功及垂成，时不再来，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1242923", 1242923, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>机难轻失</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242923_comment'></div>臣日夜料之熟矣，惟陛下图之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月21日</a>　一日得十二金字牌，遂班师。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临颍
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='41a115152c8449df923d118236cf0e05_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41a115152c8449df923d118236cf0e05");'><span id='41a115152c8449df923d118236cf0e05_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，38岁</div><div id='41a115152c8449df923d118236cf0e05' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月13日</a>　复败宗弼于临颖小商桥，上章奏捷。作品：《小商桥捷奏》<div id='poem_1242999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小商桥捷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, "宋", "岳飞", "poem_title_1242999")'>岳飞</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1242999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1242999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1242999'>武胜定国军节度使、开府仪同三司、湖北京西路宣抚使兼营田大使、河南北诸路招讨使臣岳飞状奏：今月十四日，本司前军统制、同提举一行事务张宪申：「今月十三日，统率背嵬、游奕并诸军人马，起发前来小商桥北一带，至临颍县，措置掩杀金贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1242999_comment'></div>于今月十四日天明，据<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242999", 1242999, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>绰路马</span>报，临颍县南逢金贼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1242999", 1242999, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>绰路马</span>遂追赶过县三十馀里，杀死贼兵不知数目，其贼望颍昌府、尉氏县路前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242999_comment'></div>委获胜捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242999_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1242999_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
黄冈

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月11日</a>　发鄂渚，抵黄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月15日</a>　复赐御札趣出兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月17日</a>　探知金人韩常犯蔡州，上章以闻。作品：《虏贼韩常等犯界奏》<div id='poem_1243029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243029?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上虏贼韩常等犯界事劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1243029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243029'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243029'>据德安府屯驻本司统制官庞荣申：探得蔡州除旧有番贼韩常等贼马外，又据探报，李成押千户一十五人，人马约一万五千馀骑，正月十八日已到蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243029_comment'></div>除已堤备外，奏闻事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1243029_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月21日</a>　上章乞知张俊与金人会战时间及地点，以早准备。作品：《乞检坐张俊等会战去处奏》<div id='poem_1242926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1242926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1242926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞检坐张俊等会战去处奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25061, id='poem_sentence_0_1242926_comment'></div>伏读圣训，以金贼侵犯淮西，已在庐州，张俊等并力与贼相拒，令臣提兵合击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1242926_comment'></div>或来江州，或出蕲、黄，绕出其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1242926_comment'></div>臣敢不仰体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1242926", 1242926, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>睿眷</span>，殚竭愚陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1242926_comment'></div>今日臣已抵黄州，见前去舒、蕲州界相度形势利害，看贼意向，别行措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1242926_comment'></div>不知张俊等会战在甚日，庶几臣得以照应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1242926_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1242926_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
